## 

<span key="207aa3f9533142ee8cd0749aafd21801"><span offset-key="207aa3f9533142ee8cd0749aafd21801:0">Visibility of system status</span></span>

<span key="35ca46d194014bbaba42c5cce716a488"><span offset-key="35ca46d194014bbaba42c5cce716a488:0">The system should keep users informed through appropriate feedback within reasonable time</span></span>

## 

<span key="3f9a75f1f97241e4b50094c89781a66a"><span offset-key="3f9a75f1f97241e4b50094c89781a66a:0">Match between system and the real world</span></span>

<span key="f9cd6690451742e1bb17d4f1cc3f119a"><span offset-key="f9cd6690451742e1bb17d4f1cc3f119a:0">The system should speak the users' language rather than system-oriented terms. Follow real-world conventions</span></span>

## 

<span key="b18bc24e49c24531a8002dd86dc27ec4"><span offset-key="b18bc24e49c24531a8002dd86dc27ec4:0">User control and freedom</span></span>

<span key="47c7c09faeaf4aa0832818ce9fdb29d3"><span offset-key="47c7c09faeaf4aa0832818ce9fdb29d3:0">Users often make mistakes and need 'emergency exits' to leave the unwanted state. Support undo and redo</span></span>

## 

<span key="6aefdeff369f47b8815c7a2a8c259879"><span offset-key="6aefdeff369f47b8815c7a2a8c259879:0">Consistency and standards</span></span>

<span key="06f414bd59bd4089a5cf3df9d099016b"><span offset-key="06f414bd59bd4089a5cf3df9d099016b:0">Users shouldn't have to wonder whether different words, situations, or actions mean the same thing. Follow platform conventions</span></span>

## 

<span key="4d6c6245323d46ee995a6615dc2308fa"><span offset-key="4d6c6245323d46ee995a6615dc2308fa:0">Error prevention</span></span>

<span key="c7abd475e46d4cf0909bd66624c770df"><span offset-key="c7abd475e46d4cf0909bd66624c770df:0">Prevent problems from occuring in the first place, or check for them and present users with a confirmation option before they commit to the action</span></span>

## 

<span key="87c08470cea8446e9fd9df3910834564"><span offset-key="87c08470cea8446e9fd9df3910834564:0">Recognition rather than recall</span></span>

<span key="b34f006d719c44978e1345af428b15b2"><span offset-key="b34f006d719c44978e1345af428b15b2:0">Minimize memory load by making objects, actions, and options visible. Instructions should be visible or easily retrievable</span></span>

## 

<span key="d2d06ec24c15467cae35bbd7567b0680"><span offset-key="d2d06ec24c15467cae35bbd7567b0680:0">Flexibility and efficiency of use</span></span>

<span key="702f5b92bf1a4d2b82dbcc2bb445f3ec"><span offset-key="702f5b92bf1a4d2b82dbcc2bb445f3ec:0">Accelerators - unseen by the novice user - may often speed up the interaction for the expert user. Allow users to tailor frequent actions</span></span>

## 

<span key="5966ad56846c429b9a1783cb0ef6f602"><span offset-key="5966ad56846c429b9a1783cb0ef6f602:0">Aesthetic and minimalist design</span></span>

<span key="2dbdfdde5e1943b887cd3e19273c2ccf"><span offset-key="2dbdfdde5e1943b887cd3e19273c2ccf:0">Dialogues should not contain information which is irrelevant or rarely needed</span></span>

## 

<span key="d31a9af0c3b74d229645196d2db1e450"><span offset-key="d31a9af0c3b74d229645196d2db1e450:0">Help recognize & recover from errors</span></span>

<span key="5dba9ffae4ad4d74b28bb6aa1995f072"><span offset-key="5dba9ffae4ad4d74b28bb6aa1995f072:0">Error messages should be expressed in plain language, indicate the problem, and suggest a solution</span></span>

## 

<span key="c76e06538dc748c7bdeb0695f04e0c74"><span offset-key="c76e06538dc748c7bdeb0695f04e0c74:0">Help and documentation</span></span>

<span key="cd153272bfb64c71b848a66045fd1167"><span offset-key="cd153272bfb64c71b848a66045fd1167:0">Any necessary help documentation should be easy to search, focused on the user's task, list concrete steps to be carried out, and not be too large</span></span>

<span key="1aa4e622934a41d5a55de2868867502b"><span offset-key="1aa4e622934a41d5a55de2868867502b:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="e38bdefc1cc74ed5a3a2f8d72d0e20f0"><span offset-key="e38bdefc1cc74ed5a3a2f8d72d0e20f0:0">UX Patterns</span></span>

## 

<span key="285972055b2547aba0f0fd0c06e79d52"><span offset-key="285972055b2547aba0f0fd0c06e79d52:0">UX Patterns: Modeling an Experience</span></span>

<span key="0f37e85b8422441aadb57a545b256327"><span offset-key="0f37e85b8422441aadb57a545b256327:0">Once we narrow our focus to UI/UX, the difference between a UX pattern and a UI pattern becomes subtle. Why is that?</span></span>

<span key="2be4e5c744fc42f188a3bcc60747c87e"><span offset-key="2be4e5c744fc42f188a3bcc60747c87e:0">Think about our definition of </span>*pattern*<span offset-key="2be4e5c744fc42f188a3bcc60747c87e:2">â€”a recipe for a solution to a common problem.</span></span>

<span key="ba9317eaf6ae40bb8df836c7029c45fc"><span offset-key="ba9317eaf6ae40bb8df836c7029c45fc:0">So much of what we design and build for a user experience is via a user interface. So naturally, a pattern to solve a </span>*user experience*<span offset-key="ba9317eaf6ae40bb8df836c7029c45fc:2"> problem will often involve a </span>*user interface*<span offset-key="ba9317eaf6ae40bb8df836c7029c45fc:4"> pattern.</span></span>

<span key="00440aca46b142688de7410817eccb0a"><span offset-key="00440aca46b142688de7410817eccb0a:0">But let's start by considering the general ways we can understand and start to model a user </span>*experience*<span offset-key="00440aca46b142688de7410817eccb0a:2">â€”the knowledge we have about what drives positive product experiences.</span></span>

## 

<span key="7effb223e580467cb7e231f70d5d7a6b"><span offset-key="7effb223e580467cb7e231f70d5d7a6b:0">Jakob's Law</span></span>

<span key="d3b2975a2e194194aa0733b319768734"><span offset-key="d3b2975a2e194194aa0733b319768734:0">In 2000, Jakob Nielsen of the Nielsen Norman Group </span></span><a href="https://www.nngroup.com/articles/end-of-web-design/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fbbf3a2c9a6e4cc48890a80385a4ca78" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="95f3dfd332e940d1a4b0aa8477320699"><span data-offset-key="95f3dfd332e940d1a4b0aa8477320699:0">posited (Links to an external site.)</span></span></span></a><span key="2feee80ffe844b95a42ee730939bcef2"><span offset-key="2feee80ffe844b95a42ee730939bcef2:0">:</span></span>

> <span key="5c3c4111de8d44fe87463e8b09dfca0e">**Users spend most of their time on** ***other*** **sites.**<span offset-key="5c3c4111de8d44fe87463e8b09dfca0e:3"> This means that users prefer your site to work the same way as all the other sites they already know.</span></span>

<span key="27177a3566784a48b4bdc13f835b45d1"><span offset-key="27177a3566784a48b4bdc13f835b45d1:0">Note that Nielsen isn't just talking about the way websites </span>*look*<span offset-key="27177a3566784a48b4bdc13f835b45d1:2">â€”he's referring to how they </span>*work*<span offset-key="27177a3566784a48b4bdc13f835b45d1:4">. In other words, in general, a user's experience with a website will be better if they don't have to learn new ways to interact with it. What's the takeaway here? </span>**Use UX patterns!**</span>

<span key="fe72afe2ef2c433ba7e334410f3c09d5"><span offset-key="fe72afe2ef2c433ba7e334410f3c09d5:0">Naturally, there's </span></span><a href="https://medium.cobeisfresh.com/jakobs-law-e368d03c7636" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="59ffdbedc30542aeb5d26e534f707536" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="532c619dfb39416a91f9395588691242"><span data-offset-key="532c619dfb39416a91f9395588691242:0">some controversy (Links to an external site.)</span></span></span></a><span key="48705178b7a744da87bc1197506d94f1"><span offset-key="48705178b7a744da87bc1197506d94f1:0"> about taking Jakob's Law to its absolute conclusion. If we all want users to avoid having to experience different sites differently, then will all websites end up exactly the same?</span></span>

<span key="d0dd87b766044bcf97bb2fd06881c440"><span offset-key="d0dd87b766044bcf97bb2fd06881c440:0">Nonetheless, when you're designing a product and thinking about your user's experience, it can be a very useful rule of thumb: </span>***don't reinvent the wheel***<span offset-key="d0dd87b766044bcf97bb2fd06881c440:2">. Default to the "boring" way to let your user experience your productâ€”</span>*then*<span offset-key="d0dd87b766044bcf97bb2fd06881c440:4"> think about ways to tweak that experience if it makes sense for your product's goals.</span></span>

## 

<span key="8731a83bce274a55bc5d06c0f1004cbf"><span offset-key="8731a83bce274a55bc5d06c0f1004cbf:0">The Hook Model</span></span>

<span key="195c4d5acb644848b96ba6e648626595"><span offset-key="195c4d5acb644848b96ba6e648626595:0">In his influential 2014 book </span>*Hooked: How to Build Habit-Forming Products*<span offset-key="195c4d5acb644848b96ba6e648626595:2">, Nir Eyal proposed </span></span><a href="https://www.nirandfar.com/how-to-manufacture-desire/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9d004e1477574a04ab141a0658d8e8cf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3d0fb7bc93d34ad08656015d1a0d4ada"><strong>the Hook Model (Links to an external site.)</strong></span></span></a><span key="e8a476c57b5947ee85b51e86883c8958"><span offset-key="e8a476c57b5947ee85b51e86883c8958:0">.</span></span>

<span key="aca8306d6f7842eea3292502b56f683a"><span offset-key="aca8306d6f7842eea3292502b56f683a:0">The Hook model divides a user's interaction and experience with a product into four phases:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="fdeb4437a64940d09646bd2e86b21c00"><span offset-key="fdeb4437a64940d09646bd2e86b21c00:0">A trigger to start using it</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="e7dd04125fcc44abbaa3368e6cdd8c42"><span offset-key="e7dd04125fcc44abbaa3368e6cdd8c42:0">An action that "satisfies" the trigger</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="0e42bd42b72b4b3184319553772b7d0d"><span offset-key="0e42bd42b72b4b3184319553772b7d0d:0">A reward for the action</span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="535ad41738fb41b7bfe64e8fdc1021a5"><span offset-key="535ad41738fb41b7bfe64e8fdc1021a5:0">An "investment" that makes the product more valuable to the user</span></span>

<span key="80333d119b5f4ed3ad8dcba23214604b"><span offset-key="80333d119b5f4ed3ad8dcba23214604b:0">Taken together, these phases of the Hook Model are a UX pattern. We're predicting ways that users will become engaged with our product via an experience we can engineer.</span></span>

<span key="cb576d1b86bc42c4bb798bf2dbf10e56"><span offset-key="cb576d1b86bc42c4bb798bf2dbf10e56:0">One thing to note here, howeverâ€”the Hook Model focuses on optimizing products for </span>*engagement*<span offset-key="cb576d1b86bc42c4bb798bf2dbf10e56:2">â€”it doesn't necessarily optimize products for </span>*quality*<span offset-key="cb576d1b86bc42c4bb798bf2dbf10e56:4">. In any case, though, keep it in mind as a valuable way to build a product experience that will keep users coming back.</span></span>

## 

<span key="285be814d1ca45f9bb4a3a58e04aa50e"><span offset-key="285be814d1ca45f9bb4a3a58e04aa50e:0">Gamification</span></span>

<span key="9076d5712d6c4e3ab390e88ea09309c5">**Gamification**<span offset-key="9076d5712d6c4e3ab390e88ea09309c5:1"> is incorporating game-like reward features into a product that isn't nominally a game.</span></span>

<span key="f761df9ee1a84d4d9a068898c0998077"><span offset-key="f761df9ee1a84d4d9a068898c0998077:0">One example of gamification is the Wikimedia Foundation's </span></span><a href="https://donate.wikimedia.org/wiki/Template:DonationBadges" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce5f03d23f51442d98f486bcc3a3d62c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="05854a350fdd43ebbcd41bd403fa86d9"><span data-offset-key="05854a350fdd43ebbcd41bd403fa86d9:0">donation badges (Links to an external site.)</span></span></span></a><span key="c401116ec19f4bcfbd6b3b970af749c5"><span offset-key="c401116ec19f4bcfbd6b3b970af749c5:0">â€”users who donate get recognized with a public badge (this also incorporates another useful concept: </span>**social proof**<span offset-key="c401116ec19f4bcfbd6b3b970af749c5:2">â€”giving your users examples of other people using your product in a certain way to encourage them to do so, too). Another frequent example is giving users points for completing certain actions, like filling in their profile information.</span></span>

<span key="5e316b18fcde4d74a329b1db7ad461e5"><span offset-key="5e316b18fcde4d74a329b1db7ad461e5:0">To drive positive product experiences, you'll want to ensure you're </span>**motivating**<span offset-key="5e316b18fcde4d74a329b1db7ad461e5:2"> your users, not manipulating themâ€”and that you're not relying on gamification alone to make the user experience great.</span></span>

## 

<span key="f56b97100360426d8557443adf797d7a"><span offset-key="f56b97100360426d8557443adf797d7a:0">The List Goes On...</span></span>

<span key="a2743bee2d814f2b8aa20257a0e93ca5"><span offset-key="a2743bee2d814f2b8aa20257a0e93ca5:0">There are hundreds of UX patterns out there, like:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="ee78d0e088ca4a9b980f238482b51aa2"><span offset-key="ee78d0e088ca4a9b980f238482b51aa2:0">ways to give feedback to the user</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="fdf6fbae583a44c293d248f92725c55a"><span offset-key="fdf6fbae583a44c293d248f92725c55a:0">ways to increase or decrease choices for the user</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="a9c3f3acdb7a491ab3ef6bf884d929ce"><span offset-key="a9c3f3acdb7a491ab3ef6bf884d929ce:0">ways to rely on or assist users' memory</span></span>

<span key="b6b395160af840deb7544a22bf711e0d"><span offset-key="b6b395160af840deb7544a22bf711e0d:0">If you want to read more about UX patterns, check out </span></span><a href="https://lawsofux.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="639acae410924454a1cd718578c68d7e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="75e7e32fafd248829b3020d003da2815"><strong>Laws of UX (Links to an external site.)</strong></span></span></a><span key="3a998e9626644543add336ae5b3d193d"><span offset-key="3a998e9626644543add336ae5b3d193d:0">, a really cool site laying out a bunch of research-driven UX principles and best practices.</span></span>

<span key="d81edbd8a5e4471cba0ec5020fef60fe"><span offset-key="d81edbd8a5e4471cba0ec5020fef60fe:0">We've barely scratched the surfaceâ€”but hopefully, these examples give you an idea of the work that has been done to understand user experiences, and to synthesize that knowledge into formulas for product success.</span></span>

# 

<span key="f8376bd7945f4774aad0e6900ac7b053"><span offset-key="f8376bd7945f4774aad0e6900ac7b053:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="120f916021c94398aedfebc02ba9f0c3"><span offset-key="120f916021c94398aedfebc02ba9f0c3:0">UI Patterns</span></span>

## 

<span key="07003ee20f034fd3855a82c211d49685"><span offset-key="07003ee20f034fd3855a82c211d49685:0">UI Patterns: Implementing Paradigms</span></span>

<span key="f4dc724708584cb086735e74e5700271"><span offset-key="f4dc724708584cb086735e74e5700271:0">Now that we've examined general approaches to user experience problems, we can take some of those </span>**paradigms**<span offset-key="f4dc724708584cb086735e74e5700271:2">â€”models for thinking about thingsâ€”and see how we can implement them via user interfaces.</span></span>

## 

<span key="22855a38fbcb4bd889eba9b585d921a6"><span offset-key="22855a38fbcb4bd889eba9b585d921a6:0">Common UI Patterns</span></span>

<span key="909fb90b066c4cfdad599a372ee210da"><span offset-key="909fb90b066c4cfdad599a372ee210da:0">These frequently-used UI patterns combine structure, organization, and interaction behavior to meet users where they are and provide predictable, minimum-friction experiences. You'll almost certainly immediately recognize them!</span></span>

### 

<span key="46bee48c88ab4707ae7a3571ea3fea8f"><span offset-key="46bee48c88ab4707ae7a3571ea3fea8f:0">Pagination</span></span>

<span key="fb59c6f397f24b05beb4e77716f85e98">**Pagination**<span offset-key="fb59c6f397f24b05beb4e77716f85e98:1"> is splitting content up into pages. These aren't necessary separate screens or webpagesâ€”you'll usually deal with pagination when you're working with tables:</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoyMHB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoyMHB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMjIuNjEgMTYuOTVBNSA1IDAgMDAxOCAxMGgtMS4yNmE4IDggMCAwMC03LjA1LTZNNSA1YTggOCAwIDAwNCAxNWg5YTUgNSAwIDAwMS43LS4zTTEgMWwyMiAyMiI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h" />

Could not load image

<span key="3333464655a0442fac022bead335b2c5"><span offset-key="3333464655a0442fac022bead335b2c5:0">Screen%20Shot%202021-08-29%20at%208.27.19%20PM.png</span></span>

<span key="106b8cb97dad474fba2ea91aefb83b0e"><span offset-key="106b8cb97dad474fba2ea91aefb83b0e:0">Pagination helps us avoid putting too much information in front of our users at once.</span></span>

<span key="899618232f1e4771885e3a2cfb54859e"><span offset-key="899618232f1e4771885e3a2cfb54859e:0">Note that to implement pagination, your product will often need to adjust the way it queries a databaseâ€”we'll probably only want to retrieve the "page" of data we're interested in displaying. This is called </span>**query pagination**<span offset-key="899618232f1e4771885e3a2cfb54859e:2">. Pagination is thus a great example of how designing a user interface based on a user experience can result in a full-stack engineering featureâ€”the frontend and the backend will need to accommodate paginated queries in order to present this experience to the user.</span></span>

### 

<span key="c6c4c6f2e6b74a0dbaa2c0bd7aff1a41"><span offset-key="c6c4c6f2e6b74a0dbaa2c0bd7aff1a41:0">Progressive Disclosure</span></span>

<span key="185c86ce8a994710b411a7801e13f9c4">**Progressive disclosure**<span offset-key="185c86ce8a994710b411a7801e13f9c4:1"> is waiting to show content and/or prompt the user for action until it's needed. As the user continues toward a goal, they complete the process gradually. Pagination is an example of progressive disclosure!</span></span>

<span key="4f43e0241a8d437b8d667a3cbeb1081c"><span offset-key="4f43e0241a8d437b8d667a3cbeb1081c:0">Another example of progressive disclosure is using </span>**lazy forms**<span offset-key="4f43e0241a8d437b8d667a3cbeb1081c:2">â€”forms whose fields only appear once the user has filled in the previous field (or set of fields):</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoyMHB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoyMHB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMjIuNjEgMTYuOTVBNSA1IDAgMDAxOCAxMGgtMS4yNmE4IDggMCAwMC03LjA1LTZNNSA1YTggOCAwIDAwNCAxNWg5YTUgNSAwIDAwMS43LS4zTTEgMWwyMiAyMiI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h" />

Could not load image

<span key="b160d0f1a22a44b098199aec56245c5c"><span offset-key="b160d0f1a22a44b098199aec56245c5c:0">Screen%20Shot%202021-08-29%20at%208.35.39%20PM.png</span></span>

<span key="89aa04a180634e40b293f22d5b28f883"><span offset-key="89aa04a180634e40b293f22d5b28f883:0">A related concept is using </span>**wizards**<span offset-key="89aa04a180634e40b293f22d5b28f883:2">â€”walking the user through a process, with input fields or other required actions showing over multiple pages or screens:</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoyMHB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoyMHB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMjIuNjEgMTYuOTVBNSA1IDAgMDAxOCAxMGgtMS4yNmE4IDggMCAwMC03LjA1LTZNNSA1YTggOCAwIDAwNCAxNWg5YTUgNSAwIDAwMS43LS4zTTEgMWwyMiAyMiI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h" />

Could not load image

<span key="8011f6e4ca6e408bb4414f8714c858b4"><span offset-key="8011f6e4ca6e408bb4414f8714c858b4:0">Screen%20Shot%202021-08-29%20at%208.39.19%20PM.png</span></span>

<span key="80ae66fbefe64f07a70d524318900eef"><span offset-key="80ae66fbefe64f07a70d524318900eef:0">Progressive disclosure prevents users from being intimidated by having to go through a lot of information or perform a lot of actions at once.</span></span>

### 

<span key="542abc6946ae4085a8a76beefd3d3bbf"><span offset-key="542abc6946ae4085a8a76beefd3d3bbf:0">Breadcrumbs</span></span>

<span key="fdef5432c9214b40b57aee433338fa40">**Breadcrumbs**<span offset-key="fdef5432c9214b40b57aee433338fa40:1"> are a very common UI pattern where we display a "secondary" navigation system to the user based on where they are in a hierarchy of pages or screens.</span></span>

<span key="b198f5e6d71f486d87b9a5d5af2daf5a"><span offset-key="b198f5e6d71f486d87b9a5d5af2daf5a:0">Note the breadcrumbs below (</span>`New Items`<span offset-key="b198f5e6d71f486d87b9a5d5af2daf5a:2"> â†’ </span>`Popular`<span offset-key="b198f5e6d71f486d87b9a5d5af2daf5a:4"> â†’ </span>`On Sale`<span offset-key="b198f5e6d71f486d87b9a5d5af2daf5a:6">):</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoyMHB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoyMHB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMjIuNjEgMTYuOTVBNSA1IDAgMDAxOCAxMGgtMS4yNmE4IDggMCAwMC03LjA1LTZNNSA1YTggOCAwIDAwNCAxNWg5YTUgNSAwIDAwMS43LS4zTTEgMWwyMiAyMiI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h" />

Could not load image

<span key="0411c098b0c14c818fd93fc2649ff57e"><span offset-key="0411c098b0c14c818fd93fc2649ff57e:0">Screen%20Shot%202021-08-29%20at%208.46.56%20PM.png</span></span>

<span key="138a993c9a244a239b719193da75fb79"><span offset-key="138a993c9a244a239b719193da75fb79:0">Breadcrumbs both </span>**orient the user**<span offset-key="138a993c9a244a239b719193da75fb79:2"> and allow them to </span>**navigate in context**<span offset-key="138a993c9a244a239b719193da75fb79:4">.</span></span>

<span key="a494fe57d26441379d37f2342bf6da30"><span offset-key="a494fe57d26441379d37f2342bf6da30:0">In order to be usefully orienting, breadcrumbs should be based on the actual page or screen hierarchy (the way the content is actually organized) rather than whatever way the user has happened to navigate around (their </span>**history**<span offset-key="a494fe57d26441379d37f2342bf6da30:2">). That's because showing the hierarchy gives the user more information about how your product's content is structured.</span></span>

### 

<span key="cf154b22c2d346e19126e50466f7901a"><span offset-key="cf154b22c2d346e19126e50466f7901a:0">Empty States</span></span>

<span key="72e3f0d5be90445daf3698583cb1b730">**Empty states**<span offset-key="72e3f0d5be90445daf3698583cb1b730:1"> are an extremely useful pattern that tells the user: "There's nothing here </span>*right now*<span offset-key="72e3f0d5be90445daf3698583cb1b730:3">â€”but there could be!"</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMXJhc2kzaCIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoyMHB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoyMHB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMjIuNjEgMTYuOTVBNSA1IDAgMDAxOCAxMGgtMS4yNmE4IDggMCAwMC03LjA1LTZNNSA1YTggOCAwIDAwNCAxNWg5YTUgNSAwIDAwMS43LS4zTTEgMWwyMiAyMiI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" class="r-1rasi3h" />

Could not load image

<span key="7d968c201e544f2196430f0b9ea1df5e"><span offset-key="7d968c201e544f2196430f0b9ea1df5e:0">Screen%20Shot%202021-08-29%20at%208.52.28%20PM.png</span></span>

<span key="21d9568a4e9b473a88c7bb32064a6c74"><span offset-key="21d9568a4e9b473a88c7bb32064a6c74:0">Empty states are highly orienting for users, because it tells them both how they should be interacting with your product, and what to expect both in the short term and the long term.</span></span>

<span key="be64ee51da314d08983f014fcc3ed068"><span offset-key="be64ee51da314d08983f014fcc3ed068:0">If your users will land on a screen where data </span>*could*<span offset-key="be64ee51da314d08983f014fcc3ed068:2"> be displayed, but there currently isn't anything to show themâ€”you'll </span>*almost certainly*<span offset-key="be64ee51da314d08983f014fcc3ed068:4"> want to show them an empty state.</span></span>

##

<span key="6dbcd92112b24977812432c5b88d3e67"><span offset-key="6dbcd92112b24977812432c5b88d3e67:0">There's no way we could list out all the possible UI patterns availableâ€”there are probably thousands!</span></span>

<span key="c3d38de764e74c21a06e7bcfc1193845"><span offset-key="c3d38de764e74c21a06e7bcfc1193845:0">To see more and learn more about UI patterns, check out these resources:</span></span>

# 

<span key="f59036dc0869499ba9c27e203f9e112f"><span offset-key="f59036dc0869499ba9c27e203f9e112f:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="00eea5024e0e4bd4845b80c90ef3b81a"><span offset-key="00eea5024e0e4bd4845b80c90ef3b81a:0">Accessibility:</span></span>

<span key="e35531878b084bb593e5fcd9bebe9553"><span offset-key="e35531878b084bb593e5fcd9bebe9553:0">This checklist uses </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/standards-guidelines/wcag/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="930eb5d1b895403ca0b682d5e5a64197" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="590705a0e0d5442894512fa823111cfc"><span data-offset-key="590705a0e0d5442894512fa823111cfc:0">The Web Content Accessibility Guidelines (WCAG)</span></span></span></a><span key="4d1fa6b9daa84afabe6bca3cc739eff6"><span offset-key="4d1fa6b9daa84afabe6bca3cc739eff6:0"> as a reference point. The WCAG is a shared standard for web content accessibility for individuals, organizations, and governments.</span></span>

<span key="4805ae81bee94137b8aad2d010159419"><span offset-key="4805ae81bee94137b8aad2d010159419:0">There are three levels of accessibility compliance in the WCAG, which reflect the priority of support:</span></span>

<span key="aacc817551fb45b6874c108ac9e1fab8"><span offset-key="aacc817551fb45b6874c108ac9e1fab8:0">A: EssentialIf this isn't met, assistive technology may not be able to read, understand, or fully operate the page or view.</span></span>

<span key="42ac66391f6147a4bef48146371af42f"><span offset-key="42ac66391f6147a4bef48146371af42f:0">AA: Ideal SupportRequired for </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/policies/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb54fafaf5eb4838b5464c1eda03ed6c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="adab0246e09d4edf8ce662f000e63579"><span data-offset-key="adab0246e09d4edf8ce662f000e63579:0">multiple government and public body websites</span></span></span></a><span key="6d94beca602844d49e15ffbce5f001a5"><span offset-key="6d94beca602844d49e15ffbce5f001a5:0">. The A11Y Project strives for AA compliance.</span></span>

<span key="b4a1e0a0fd1f4ebdaa540af0c93fd6f2"><span offset-key="b4a1e0a0fd1f4ebdaa540af0c93fd6f2:0">AAA: Specialized SupportThis is typically reserved for parts of websites and web apps that serve a specialized audience.</span></span>

<span key="061de9891bd64dea8d977b4d78d69aed"><span offset-key="061de9891bd64dea8d977b4d78d69aed:0">This checklist targets many, but not all level A and AA concerns. Note that the different levels of WCAG support do not necessarily indicate an increased level of difficulty to implement.</span></span>

## 

<span key="b44c819e2b9c4a16b6eedb66b9f29a4b"><span offset-key="b44c819e2b9c4a16b6eedb66b9f29a4b:0">Success criteria</span></span>

<span key="aab185530bec495a83f8c9687709a385"><span offset-key="aab185530bec495a83f8c9687709a385:0">Each item on this checklist has a corresponding WCAG "success criterion." Success criterion are the specific, testable rules that power the WCAG, described by a reference number and short title. For example, the rule about text resizing is called </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-scale.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a96f9b84a4f14fdfbc593f170f3e465b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d9e1d50e23ed420b8ebffe2a7efc0713"><span data-offset-key="d9e1d50e23ed420b8ebffe2a7efc0713:0">1.4.4 Resize text</span></span></span></a><span key="92c658b0b8244f20af2c751cf8f5190e"><span offset-key="92c658b0b8244f20af2c751cf8f5190e:0">.</span></span>

<span key="ab3bbb37932f44359d318ba3e2fbbf31"><span offset-key="ab3bbb37932f44359d318ba3e2fbbf31:0">Some accessibility issues may have multiple success criterion apply to them. We have identified the one most relevant for each checklist item.</span></span>

## 

<span key="dabd2df8d5e243b4ba3a105e1c878221"><span offset-key="dabd2df8d5e243b4ba3a105e1c878221:0">Does this checklist guarantee my site is accessible?</span></span>

<span key="5ad65de55fef454687d5e1c6255574f2"><span offset-key="5ad65de55fef454687d5e1c6255574f2:0">No. However, addressing the issues called out in this checklist will help improve the experience for everyone who uses your site.</span></span>

<span key="21b938e15f444683bc385ba815f7c16b"><span offset-key="21b938e15f444683bc385ba815f7c16b:0">The issues this checklist prompts you to check for covers a wide range of disability conditions. There is no such thing as "perfect accessibility" or a site being "100% accessible." You should be wary of companies and services that make such promises. If you need professional accessibility help, use </span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/resources/#professional-help" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7265c35e01b1434392fc163bd964bbe5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="4bac2238ced649b3b631be0596711c5a"><span data-offset-key="4bac2238ced649b3b631be0596711c5a:0">professional accessibility services</span></span></span></a><span key="75840c1cbfc74ad6ba374efeba45aa1b"><span offset-key="75840c1cbfc74ad6ba374efeba45aa1b:0">.</span></span>

## 

<span key="6663d347efec47eeabbfc1f487aea268"><span offset-key="6663d347efec47eeabbfc1f487aea268:0">Content</span></span>

<span key="ba5d5cbc5d1e43f0aa6c5d3ed32ed69d"><span offset-key="ba5d5cbc5d1e43f0aa6c5d3ed32ed69d:0">Content is the most important part of your site.</span></span>

<span key="c46e9b3c4ada4380a1869a0bea78d241"><span offset-key="c46e9b3c4ada4380a1869a0bea78d241:0">Task: Use plain language and avoid figures of speech, idioms, and complicated metaphors.</span></span>

<span key="3a10650a06174cecaff87107a6181864"><span offset-key="3a10650a06174cecaff87107a6181864:0">Use plain language and avoid figures of speech, idioms, and complicated metaphors.</span></span>

<span key="595996f5c65944358cbe448dc399e103"><span offset-key="595996f5c65944358cbe448dc399e103:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/meaning-supplements.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1f780cd5fc6c4828a48b4e21899e8975" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="6191e90129c44c3aba2b75645f7d03da"><span data-offset-key="6191e90129c44c3aba2b75645f7d03da:0">3.1.5 READING LEVEL</span></span></span></a><span key="8e09bd73608c4e30abefb573c4866b16"><span offset-key="8e09bd73608c4e30abefb573c4866b16:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="375c4f86f7414c8faf6a4e69f358a30d"><span offset-key="375c4f86f7414c8faf6a4e69f358a30d:0">Write content at </span></span><a href="https://datayze.com/readability-analyzer.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="522a0c09490b41c8a5cb5110e0a46a4d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="be3c2cb05e8c4b9ca7d086870ff93e45"><span data-offset-key="be3c2cb05e8c4b9ca7d086870ff93e45:0">an 8th grade reading level</span></span></span></a><span key="b4a28c710bf54de79172fe77a5357c64"><span offset-key="b4a28c710bf54de79172fe77a5357c64:0">.</span></span>

<span key="b649e691a8714cbca8eb7285fb4a680d"><span offset-key="b649e691a8714cbca8eb7285fb4a680d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-plain-language-and-avoid-figures-of-speech-idioms-and-complicated-metaphors" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f61da8fd53954e5f8ca2a152357eecf3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="62440f41c7bb460bbdcb9a7a6347436a"><span data-offset-key="62440f41c7bb460bbdcb9a7a6347436a:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE PLAIN LANGUAGE AND AVOID FIGURES OF SPEECH, IDIOMS, AND COMPLICATED METAPHORS.</span></span></span></a><span key="d434e76827574d82969d4c3be889bbb3"><span offset-key="d434e76827574d82969d4c3be889bbb3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="7b21165b94a94d91a38e4f5bd900637f"><span offset-key="7b21165b94a94d91a38e4f5bd900637f:0">Task: Make sure that </span>`button`<span offset-key="7b21165b94a94d91a38e4f5bd900637f:2">, </span>`a`<span offset-key="7b21165b94a94d91a38e4f5bd900637f:4">, and </span>`label`<span offset-key="7b21165b94a94d91a38e4f5bd900637f:6"> element content is unique and descriptive.</span></span>

<span key="7c2915316faf441aa137d491376f5623"><span offset-key="7c2915316faf441aa137d491376f5623:0">Make sure that </span>`button`<span offset-key="7c2915316faf441aa137d491376f5623:2">, </span>`a`<span offset-key="7c2915316faf441aa137d491376f5623:4">, and </span>`label`<span offset-key="7c2915316faf441aa137d491376f5623:6"> element content is unique and descriptive.</span></span>

<span key="1261074a67a9403ab293ee6e5fe40cf4"><span offset-key="1261074a67a9403ab293ee6e5fe40cf4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d24f5707049846f982ba8e04a50e7368" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="092bac47f1be4f888c07ffdc6ef4629c"><span data-offset-key="092bac47f1be4f888c07ffdc6ef4629c:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="d5045532e08f452086588ae26fbe2be0"><span offset-key="d5045532e08f452086588ae26fbe2be0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="dfc769def4794d1098a3ceb0e83e8b03"><span offset-key="dfc769def4794d1098a3ceb0e83e8b03:0">Terms like "click here" and "read more" do not provide any context. Some people navigate using a list of all buttons or links on a page or view. When using this mode, the terms indicate what will happen if navigated to or activated.</span></span>

<span key="7915d343e0f04c1fad177f49bb8b5bc4"><span offset-key="7915d343e0f04c1fad177f49bb8b5bc4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-button-a-and-label-element-content-is-unique-and-descriptive" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a750394cf64f461ba648dc389ec47930" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb"><span data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:1">BUTTON</code><span data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:2">, </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:3">A</code><span data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:4">, AND </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:5">LABEL</code><span data-offset-key="07fc1b24c7484fdbbeee56ee3724b3fb:6"> ELEMENT CONTENT IS UNIQUE AND DESCRIPTIVE.</span></span></span></a><span key="3cafa07dc3e2431b8a5735782d7d258a"><span offset-key="3cafa07dc3e2431b8a5735782d7d258a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="1af33057766a46118c372501213fe634"><span offset-key="1af33057766a46118c372501213fe634:0">Task: Use left-aligned text for left-to-right (LTR) languages, and right-aligned text for right-to-left (RTL) languages.</span></span>

<span key="6a8fbbfe66a9401cb9898b5a53d5a1ed"><span offset-key="6a8fbbfe66a9401cb9898b5a53d5a1ed:0">Use left-aligned text for left-to-right (LTR) languages, and right-aligned text for right-to-left (RTL) languages.</span></span>

<span key="8acfe0af838c444b809336eacce8100e"><span offset-key="8acfe0af838c444b809336eacce8100e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-visual-presentation.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="21fb9caa19fa4f6c958d937ba9b7f59a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="8835e6dfd02247e6850ae107a93cfab9"><span data-offset-key="8835e6dfd02247e6850ae107a93cfab9:0">1.4.8 VISUAL PRESENTATION</span></span></span></a><span key="f0faa67890624a3fb486288d7e257247"><span offset-key="f0faa67890624a3fb486288d7e257247:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="6a74fc615a7841b9a6e7d3aa1fffd306"><span offset-key="6a74fc615a7841b9a6e7d3aa1fffd306:0">Centered-aligned or justified text is difficult to read.</span></span>

<span key="4c679d52df19458b974b2447ed298d1e"><span offset-key="4c679d52df19458b974b2447ed298d1e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-left-aligned-text-for-left-to-right-ltr-languages-and-right-aligned-text-for-right-to-left-rtl-languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ea0a727b9fa144dba4ca3a3abdf21d33" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="c57acb9abdaf4aba990dc6c33818d3b3"><span data-offset-key="c57acb9abdaf4aba990dc6c33818d3b3:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE LEFT-ALIGNED TEXT FOR LEFT-TO-RIGHT (LTR) LANGUAGES, AND RIGHT-ALIGNED TEXT FOR RIGHT-TO-LEFT (RTL) LANGUAGES.</span></span></span></a><span key="10824f1312b54db8bfec13649ec43940"><span offset-key="10824f1312b54db8bfec13649ec43940:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="6b5e322e432b4133af0ceaf92775e244"><span offset-key="6b5e322e432b4133af0ceaf92775e244:0">Global code</span></span>

<span key="14fd0ded59ed4cb0a2cc40ff2cf25be7"><span offset-key="14fd0ded59ed4cb0a2cc40ff2cf25be7:0">Global code is code that affects your entire website or web app.</span></span>

<span key="2136ea871f7c44b7807a2bae04d6cd2b"><span offset-key="2136ea871f7c44b7807a2bae04d6cd2b:0">Task: Validate your HTML.</span></span>

<span key="e28c7d1815be4f82ae20aadfc22902a1"><span offset-key="e28c7d1815be4f82ae20aadfc22902a1:0">Validate your HTML.</span></span>

<span key="06e77f02cdf745899b971616868209e2"><span offset-key="06e77f02cdf745899b971616868209e2:0">Task: Use a </span>`lang`<span offset-key="06e77f02cdf745899b971616868209e2:2"> attribute on the </span>`html`<span offset-key="06e77f02cdf745899b971616868209e2:4"> element.</span></span>

<span key="550c2cba51b0497bbacb440c36816136"><span offset-key="550c2cba51b0497bbacb440c36816136:0">Use a </span>`lang`<span offset-key="550c2cba51b0497bbacb440c36816136:2"> attribute on the </span>`html`<span offset-key="550c2cba51b0497bbacb440c36816136:4"> element.</span></span>

<span key="112edb19263641258dd594974bece6f4"><span offset-key="112edb19263641258dd594974bece6f4:0">Task: Provide a unique </span>`title`<span offset-key="112edb19263641258dd594974bece6f4:2"> for each page or view.</span></span>

<span key="4d6ad667d43144468b70c806eb159b07"><span offset-key="4d6ad667d43144468b70c806eb159b07:0">Provide a unique </span>`title`<span offset-key="4d6ad667d43144468b70c806eb159b07:2"> for each page or view.</span></span>

<span key="c0f7602001e644abaa762428b58241e8"><span offset-key="c0f7602001e644abaa762428b58241e8:0">Task: Ensure that viewport zoom is not disabled.</span></span>

<span key="7e51a730c0fd4a25a607b467ea2c96cb"><span offset-key="7e51a730c0fd4a25a607b467ea2c96cb:0">Ensure that viewport zoom is not disabled.</span></span>

<span key="0ea5b3871a8342928802f44b7abecf47"><span offset-key="0ea5b3871a8342928802f44b7abecf47:0">Task: Use landmark elements to indicate important content regions.</span></span>

<span key="97c1ef24d602416d9a9501ec8fd3c611"><span offset-key="97c1ef24d602416d9a9501ec8fd3c611:0">Use landmark elements to indicate important content regions.</span></span>

<span key="10cf4e828b75475983f776af3ce8fbae"><span offset-key="10cf4e828b75475983f776af3ce8fbae:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/ensure-compat-rsv.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="699d5b8babfb46e982799c7170df0133" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="b47f026f687948b4827f7e6bef1f87a6"><span data-offset-key="b47f026f687948b4827f7e6bef1f87a6:0">4.1.2 NAME, ROLE, VALUE</span></span></span></a><span key="e87439f0220a409e8e9ef8d815d573ac"><span offset-key="e87439f0220a409e8e9ef8d815d573ac:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="dc41e6457ae6407b956bad20e87da31a"><span offset-key="dc41e6457ae6407b956bad20e87da31a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices/examples/landmarks/HTML5.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="92cc006a01994f0589c39c898d5d6fa7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ef7291bac2ca468faf70e18b39800003"><span data-offset-key="ef7291bac2ca468faf70e18b39800003:0">Landmark regions</span></span></span></a><span key="4b00264d670a4dd68d9e4a442f6a292c"><span offset-key="4b00264d670a4dd68d9e4a442f6a292c:0"> help communicate the layout and important areas of a page or view, and can allow quick access to these regions. For example, use the </span>`nav`<span offset-key="4b00264d670a4dd68d9e4a442f6a292c:2"> element to wrap a site's navigation, and the </span>`main`<span offset-key="4b00264d670a4dd68d9e4a442f6a292c:4"> element to contain the primary content of a page.</span></span>

<span key="ae9ea33317824e3f89d1abe5044ecc2e"><span offset-key="ae9ea33317824e3f89d1abe5044ecc2e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-landmark-elements-to-indicate-important-content-regions" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c024e123322d4d689969759c58e77296" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="1e5c502f3e1245e38fb56e07cb8ee4eb"><span data-offset-key="1e5c502f3e1245e38fb56e07cb8ee4eb:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE LANDMARK ELEMENTS TO INDICATE IMPORTANT CONTENT REGIONS.</span></span></span></a><span key="3fb7d727768f4c16af8e1beaa3b41ebb"><span offset-key="3fb7d727768f4c16af8e1beaa3b41ebb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="71b4c5d3f0b947c9a68134cc2ce9074e"><span offset-key="71b4c5d3f0b947c9a68134cc2ce9074e:0">Task: Ensure a linear content flow.</span></span>

<span key="b5e3322b1326470d865d0722f7f76b7c"><span offset-key="b5e3322b1326470d865d0722f7f76b7c:0">Ensure a linear content flow.</span></span>

<span key="965c893078da4c6cb176fa087db607e4"><span offset-key="965c893078da4c6cb176fa087db607e4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-focus-order.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4dfa90417a5b48499513a306f5638787" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d400ac8c943241adb517ca7bba16ed7a"><span data-offset-key="d400ac8c943241adb517ca7bba16ed7a:0">2.4.3 FOCUS ORDER</span></span></span></a><span key="45d801e6ab0f4382bc17b62cb3b1c811"><span offset-key="45d801e6ab0f4382bc17b62cb3b1c811:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0"><span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:0">Remove </span>`tabindex`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:2"> attribute values that aren't either </span>`0`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:4"> or </span>`-1`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:6">. Elements that are inherently focusable, such as links or </span>`button`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:8"> elements, do not require a </span>`tabindex`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:10">. Elements that are not inherently focusable should not have a </span>`tabindex`<span offset-key="a6296bfcd7cd483e963d406a20b50ec0:12"> applied to them outside of very specific use cases.</span></span>

<span key="acf92d5ecef94fb4abcc222f19397764"><span offset-key="acf92d5ecef94fb4abcc222f19397764:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-a-linear-content-flow" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6af080405a5c4c389b82bd3f0f96fe3d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ed584da8afe745f5b71d47be2ca2f239"><span data-offset-key="ed584da8afe745f5b71d47be2ca2f239:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE A LINEAR CONTENT FLOW.</span></span></span></a><span key="e21161810ff14e12a3b463b4d174e9d7"><span offset-key="e21161810ff14e12a3b463b4d174e9d7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="294490cc7c5645f8a1b53ac6c27f7888"><span offset-key="294490cc7c5645f8a1b53ac6c27f7888:0">Task: Avoid using the </span>`autofocus`<span offset-key="294490cc7c5645f8a1b53ac6c27f7888:2"> attribute.</span></span>

<span key="f35e7b4e48e347d891ffff11141bbc82"><span offset-key="f35e7b4e48e347d891ffff11141bbc82:0">Avoid using the </span>`autofocus`<span offset-key="f35e7b4e48e347d891ffff11141bbc82:2"> attribute.</span></span>

<span key="1bd86c1a164b4176a7882e0250ef0734"><span offset-key="1bd86c1a164b4176a7882e0250ef0734:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-focus-order.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d767202a99dd4827946212527e9eb113" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="9db4ac2bcc7143f1b5b45ee8608dd510"><span data-offset-key="9db4ac2bcc7143f1b5b45ee8608dd510:0">2.4.3 FOCUS ORDER</span></span></span></a><span key="61ce69682ff44d3284b0e0a2cd954fad"><span offset-key="61ce69682ff44d3284b0e0a2cd954fad:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="73a144fce2b0491a81bf865098d47718"><span offset-key="73a144fce2b0491a81bf865098d47718:0">People who are blind or who have low vision may be disoriented when focus is moved without their permission. Additionally, </span>`autofocus`<span offset-key="73a144fce2b0491a81bf865098d47718:2"> can be problematic for people with motor control disabilities, as it may create extra work for them to navigate out from the autofocused area and to other locations on the page/view.</span></span>

<span key="460ed236abe3499c951e8b36745dd543"><span offset-key="460ed236abe3499c951e8b36745dd543:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#avoid-using-the-autofocus-attribute" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a0eb4e40c11947baa850990c9e515217" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="e1465dd12b5c4846a86620822bee0b30"><span data-offset-key="e1465dd12b5c4846a86620822bee0b30:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: AVOID USING THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="e1465dd12b5c4846a86620822bee0b30:1">AUTOFOCUS</code><span data-offset-key="e1465dd12b5c4846a86620822bee0b30:2"> ATTRIBUTE.</span></span></span></a><span key="a140adf9d597475bb185f909a7d41378"><span offset-key="a140adf9d597475bb185f909a7d41378:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="161c161fa81446dc918b17ab7ce19696"><span offset-key="161c161fa81446dc918b17ab7ce19696:0">Task: Allow extending session timeouts</span></span>

<span key="2eba9da9ee4b499e8552ec863ce4f60d"><span offset-key="2eba9da9ee4b499e8552ec863ce4f60d:0">Allow extending session timeouts</span></span>

<span key="79b8998da01c4ba9ab8ca9341e7d1000"><span offset-key="79b8998da01c4ba9ab8ca9341e7d1000:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/time-limits-required-behaviors.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8152e2acf8b24c639e5915925bb8cd01" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="f5a0085a10ae466ab991be577a734f8c"><span data-offset-key="f5a0085a10ae466ab991be577a734f8c:0">2.2.1 TIMING ADJUSTABLE</span></span></span></a><span key="7c75d375bfaa437faa01d78ce94bbfaa"><span offset-key="7c75d375bfaa437faa01d78ce94bbfaa:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b81e4dd38e5940068c56d54b8254931e"><span offset-key="b81e4dd38e5940068c56d54b8254931e:0">If you cannot remove session timeouts altogether, then let the person using your site easily turn off, adjust, or extend their session well before it ends.</span></span>

<span key="9a93b490c6b74a3ebb5b9ff9b2a45ab7"><span offset-key="9a93b490c6b74a3ebb5b9ff9b2a45ab7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#allow-extending-session-timeouts" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c23c7e210d154a22ab0a02e7c9bcf554" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="6324470952ff4de69b5bbdd816c7d920"><span data-offset-key="6324470952ff4de69b5bbdd816c7d920:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ALLOW EXTENDING SESSION TIMEOUTS</span></span></span></a><span key="575476c7cae944f0a66fa944819ea294"><span offset-key="575476c7cae944f0a66fa944819ea294:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="84d2235e16624cd5a5f319cd78a7f710"><span offset-key="84d2235e16624cd5a5f319cd78a7f710:0">Task: Remove </span>`title`<span offset-key="84d2235e16624cd5a5f319cd78a7f710:2"> attribute tooltips.</span></span>

<span key="4f217b024b8a45c9b5d3bb85cb2c223a"><span offset-key="4f217b024b8a45c9b5d3bb85cb2c223a:0">Remove </span>`title`<span offset-key="4f217b024b8a45c9b5d3bb85cb2c223a:2"> attribute tooltips.</span></span>

<span key="219ba1e780724873a5067a81739c35fb"><span offset-key="219ba1e780724873a5067a81739c35fb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/ensure-compat-rsv.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2267586545a44e4f9a0e6ced92b96f02" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7a86e8c924074036a33f35a00279781a"><span data-offset-key="7a86e8c924074036a33f35a00279781a:0">4.1.2 NAME, ROLE, VALUE</span></span></span></a><span key="c62fba73c5bc4d708f9b3fdbc2b9c309"><span offset-key="c62fba73c5bc4d708f9b3fdbc2b9c309:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="9cd1dfa9cbca48eea86766af82d67541"><span offset-key="9cd1dfa9cbca48eea86766af82d67541:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Global_attributes/title#Accessibility_concerns" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="06d946cb51af47439d828a930050b27e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ef21f7994d0a4a2a9d2754334041149a"><span data-offset-key="ef21f7994d0a4a2a9d2754334041149a:0">The </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="ef21f7994d0a4a2a9d2754334041149a:1">title</code><span data-offset-key="ef21f7994d0a4a2a9d2754334041149a:2"> attribute has numerous issues</span></span></span></a><span key="c98db2b915af48d9a6c729ea27d6ca9e"><span offset-key="c98db2b915af48d9a6c729ea27d6ca9e:0">, and should not be used if the information provided is important for all people to access. An acceptable use for the </span>`title`<span offset-key="c98db2b915af48d9a6c729ea27d6ca9e:2"> attribute would be labeling an </span>`iframe`<span offset-key="c98db2b915af48d9a6c729ea27d6ca9e:4"> element to indicate what content it contains.</span></span>

<span key="b17d4872d82349729210dadc4e6c960f"><span offset-key="b17d4872d82349729210dadc4e6c960f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#remove-title-attribute-tooltips" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aa267c44303b44e19a0ae8fa8ae687ab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3e553f8cb7954f5e8631dea3b66d1304"><span data-offset-key="3e553f8cb7954f5e8631dea3b66d1304:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: REMOVE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3e553f8cb7954f5e8631dea3b66d1304:1">TITLE</code><span data-offset-key="3e553f8cb7954f5e8631dea3b66d1304:2"> ATTRIBUTE TOOLTIPS.</span></span></span></a><span key="822b8c108cd44d829bd4c63eba5fa2b5"><span offset-key="822b8c108cd44d829bd4c63eba5fa2b5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="8960070b666c49c6b6a61285f4b957cc"><span offset-key="8960070b666c49c6b6a61285f4b957cc:0">Keyboard</span></span>

<span key="821e3a21d5f84c5ca6736b285e8db73e"><span offset-key="821e3a21d5f84c5ca6736b285e8db73e:0">It is important that your interface and content can be operated, and navigated by use of a keyboard. Some people cannot use a mouse, or may be using other assistive technologies that may not allow for hovering or precise clicking.</span></span>

<span key="b5030e2b9ebc4aeaa387d08e1ffc09a8"><span offset-key="b5030e2b9ebc4aeaa387d08e1ffc09a8:0">Task: Make sure there is a visible focus style for interactive elements that are navigated to via keyboard input.</span></span>

<span key="74e338c22aed4c6696efa58c8414e48a"><span offset-key="74e338c22aed4c6696efa58c8414e48a:0">Make sure there is a visible focus style for interactive elements that are navigated to via keyboard input.</span></span>

<span key="3991e2ff4ddd49dbac5c0a5e233ae715"><span offset-key="3991e2ff4ddd49dbac5c0a5e233ae715:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-focus-visible.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ee7c0595ab55484b9048700681c0a4a1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="b37ff93d07964adeb5e13eddffa7b1ef"><span data-offset-key="b37ff93d07964adeb5e13eddffa7b1ef:0">2.4.7 FOCUS VISIBLE</span></span></span></a><span key="4fb97ad328ef4258a7ed03b3f229fd2f"><span offset-key="4fb97ad328ef4258a7ed03b3f229fd2f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="712b9ce069f3429786983088f5fed84c"><span offset-key="712b9ce069f3429786983088f5fed84c:0">Can a person navigating with a keyboard, </span></span><a href="https://axesslab.com/switches/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9a84458e7578483d9b75e055697c49de" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="8313d9e5130646a39c543ae5ce53fe86"><span data-offset-key="8313d9e5130646a39c543ae5ce53fe86:0">switch</span></span></span></a><span key="679076d48ddf493eb2812bf2f8a9477d"><span offset-key="679076d48ddf493eb2812bf2f8a9477d:0">, voice control, or screen reader see where they currently are on the page?</span></span>

<span key="1ad3adc9a0744c30956514d22a9eb68f"><span offset-key="1ad3adc9a0744c30956514d22a9eb68f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-there-is-a-visible-focus-style-for-interactive-elements-that-are-navigated-to-via-keyboard-input" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="db6ec5c7624143fea57ca382fb1f8ec0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="e4dc31b62abb4bd7af9e918f8a2a1f47"><span data-offset-key="e4dc31b62abb4bd7af9e918f8a2a1f47:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THERE IS A VISIBLE FOCUS STYLE FOR INTERACTIVE ELEMENTS THAT ARE NAVIGATED TO VIA KEYBOARD INPUT.</span></span></span></a><span key="bbe17299e63c45438f936051020d32d2"><span offset-key="bbe17299e63c45438f936051020d32d2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="2c976ed7af5f4a78927690c7e2e6045e"><span offset-key="2c976ed7af5f4a78927690c7e2e6045e:0">Task: Check to see that keyboard focus order matches the visual layout.</span></span>

<span key="ba76e3d0a96949d2a51350592202f441"><span offset-key="ba76e3d0a96949d2a51350592202f441:0">Check to see that keyboard focus order matches the visual layout.</span></span>

<span key="5dd7ea1599304896b67aa65417028891"><span offset-key="5dd7ea1599304896b67aa65417028891:0">Task: Remove invisible focusable elements.</span></span>

<span key="3fe8c260e43043d6b38e4ce31170deb3"><span offset-key="3fe8c260e43043d6b38e4ce31170deb3:0">Remove invisible focusable elements.</span></span>

## 

<span key="463de2bda07f47fe977534bb69622e1a"><span offset-key="463de2bda07f47fe977534bb69622e1a:0">Images</span></span>

<span key="5d4698de57fc4449947016277d2dc3c5"><span offset-key="5d4698de57fc4449947016277d2dc3c5:0">Images are a very common part of most websites. Help make sure they can be enjoyed by all.</span></span>

<span key="a4aa76db5cdc491ba2bf5736feb2b029"><span offset-key="a4aa76db5cdc491ba2bf5736feb2b029:0">Task: Make sure that all </span>`img`<span offset-key="a4aa76db5cdc491ba2bf5736feb2b029:2"> elements have an </span>`alt`<span offset-key="a4aa76db5cdc491ba2bf5736feb2b029:4"> attribute.</span></span>

<span key="8eaec4da46c248eaaed8ecc612222ec3"><span offset-key="8eaec4da46c248eaaed8ecc612222ec3:0">Make sure that all </span>`img`<span offset-key="8eaec4da46c248eaaed8ecc612222ec3:2"> elements have an </span>`alt`<span offset-key="8eaec4da46c248eaaed8ecc612222ec3:4"> attribute.</span></span>

<span key="f046018b49364fff9404c585371cdcf3"><span offset-key="f046018b49364fff9404c585371cdcf3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/text-equiv-all.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cf6f818424b4406b8be87d42db5591aa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="50f68da044164b0080733a341bebe6ad"><span data-offset-key="50f68da044164b0080733a341bebe6ad:0">1.1.1 NON-TEXT CONTENT</span></span></span></a><span key="020422a5ef9b40398ec0b4a2534cc38e"><span offset-key="020422a5ef9b40398ec0b4a2534cc38e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="32ebb00f00da43a48e2454e099e156dc">`alt`<span offset-key="32ebb00f00da43a48e2454e099e156dc:1"> attributes (alt text) give a description of an image for people who may not be able to view them. When an </span>`alt`<span offset-key="32ebb00f00da43a48e2454e099e156dc:3"> attribute isn't present on an image, a screen reader may announce the image's file name and path instead. This fails to communicate the image's content.</span></span>

<span key="9d5e5592dc6947dd97468977a514b08b"><span offset-key="9d5e5592dc6947dd97468977a514b08b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-all-img-elements-have-an-alt-attribute" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="26778dd33cba46da8c73d7f12b394567" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23"><span data-offset-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT ALL </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23:1">IMG</code><span data-offset-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23:2"> ELEMENTS HAVE AN </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23:3">ALT</code><span data-offset-key="0e206ecefce24d1883c9bc89351ebe23:4"> ATTRIBUTE.</span></span></span></a><span key="644f3305b8db4fe690bd4a149f0817ca"><span offset-key="644f3305b8db4fe690bd4a149f0817ca:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="144c8f68f59748fab93336eeb82504cc"><span offset-key="144c8f68f59748fab93336eeb82504cc:0">Task: Make sure that decorative images use null </span>`alt`<span offset-key="144c8f68f59748fab93336eeb82504cc:2"> (empty) attribute values.</span></span>

<span key="af891b2bcf044e81adb7afc913438f62"><span offset-key="af891b2bcf044e81adb7afc913438f62:0">Make sure that decorative images use null </span>`alt`<span offset-key="af891b2bcf044e81adb7afc913438f62:2"> (empty) attribute values.</span></span>

<span key="a5c849acb9ed466195fd987d00ff0fc4"><span offset-key="a5c849acb9ed466195fd987d00ff0fc4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/text-equiv-all.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="90eeb5fd9b9644d8bc5aa3aa1deb6f9e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="54dea1cb5d3e446f9fe2b95e80c73681"><span data-offset-key="54dea1cb5d3e446f9fe2b95e80c73681:0">1.1.1 NON-TEXT CONTENT</span></span></span></a><span key="c19aa565a3e34b08b6bb898a25451e5e"><span offset-key="c19aa565a3e34b08b6bb898a25451e5e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="0046834a77584fe59592d8aa74c50d8e"><span offset-key="0046834a77584fe59592d8aa74c50d8e:0">Null </span>`alt`<span offset-key="0046834a77584fe59592d8aa74c50d8e:2"> attributes are also sometimes known as empty </span>`alt`<span offset-key="0046834a77584fe59592d8aa74c50d8e:4"> attributes. They are made by including no information between the opening and closing quotes of an </span>`alt`<span offset-key="0046834a77584fe59592d8aa74c50d8e:6"> attribute. Decorative images do not communicate information that is required to understand the website's overall meaning. Historically they were used for flourishes and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spacer_GIF" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d39bd1cd47274b3ab8bbb95f3a02e06c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d2ede77119ff49a6bd4dc84c9027822a"><span data-offset-key="d2ede77119ff49a6bd4dc84c9027822a:0">spacer gif</span></span></span></a><span key="f5ac6037ff284e8bb42a45e54256cf37"><span offset-key="f5ac6037ff284e8bb42a45e54256cf37:0"> images, but tend to be less relevant for modern websites and web apps.</span></span>

<span key="142d2b88faca47e883cfbeaf5c75f654"><span offset-key="142d2b88faca47e883cfbeaf5c75f654:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-decorative-images-use-null-alt-empty-attribute-values" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5ec140c0fa9f46d4923c58b465120b70" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a1e0d0081cb6424c89f21979ec45e71b"><span data-offset-key="a1e0d0081cb6424c89f21979ec45e71b:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT DECORATIVE IMAGES USE NULL </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="a1e0d0081cb6424c89f21979ec45e71b:1">ALT</code><span data-offset-key="a1e0d0081cb6424c89f21979ec45e71b:2"> (EMPTY) ATTRIBUTE VALUES.</span></span></span></a><span key="229cf1aa198746f7baff4e8315851684"><span offset-key="229cf1aa198746f7baff4e8315851684:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="d64a4e90b8e7439fb3e73a13b1cb8d41"><span offset-key="d64a4e90b8e7439fb3e73a13b1cb8d41:0">Task: Provide a text alternative for complex images such as charts, graphs, and maps.</span></span>

<span key="4824bd4b75a744868b2aef0747111e61"><span offset-key="4824bd4b75a744868b2aef0747111e61:0">Provide a text alternative for complex images such as charts, graphs, and maps.</span></span>

<span key="7bd0363a5a3a48d99b42df365aca6c3f"><span offset-key="7bd0363a5a3a48d99b42df365aca6c3f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/text-equiv-all.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="698486b962bc416db15b3e5963dacfd1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="61222b27552448dfaaaffe92b40c44fa"><span data-offset-key="61222b27552448dfaaaffe92b40c44fa:0">1.1.1 NON-TEXT CONTENT</span></span></span></a><span key="86070879d6d243bb9e4af6ae6118eebd"><span offset-key="86070879d6d243bb9e4af6ae6118eebd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="e8e883520eb74afc8fadfd8a57cb49b2"><span offset-key="e8e883520eb74afc8fadfd8a57cb49b2:0">Is there a plain text which lists points on the map or sections of a flowchart? Describe all visible information. This includes graph axes, data points and labels, and the overall point the graphic is communicating.</span></span>

<span key="c138c460113848be9f390474b2c27041"><span offset-key="c138c460113848be9f390474b2c27041:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#provide-a-text-alternative-for-complex-images-such-as-charts-graphs-and-maps" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6e6694460b9d4a5b8d3ca956bef575b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="90aae689599140408d82ccb5a4e7e796"><span data-offset-key="90aae689599140408d82ccb5a4e7e796:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: PROVIDE A TEXT ALTERNATIVE FOR COMPLEX IMAGES SUCH AS CHARTS, GRAPHS, AND MAPS.</span></span></span></a><span key="cea763a308844ec0a7fb0ceb5d81db92"><span offset-key="cea763a308844ec0a7fb0ceb5d81db92:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="58391ee1bc25424fa007eebcabced317"><span offset-key="58391ee1bc25424fa007eebcabced317:0">Task: For images containing text, make sure the alt description includes the image's text.</span></span>

<span key="fb2dfc6da63f4ea9aad3d1433189674c"><span offset-key="fb2dfc6da63f4ea9aad3d1433189674c:0">For images containing text, make sure the alt description includes the image's text.</span></span>

<span key="71009fce73e04f0d926d4bc74bda6466"><span offset-key="71009fce73e04f0d926d4bc74bda6466:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/text-equiv-all.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3053abafcba042b0bef6887d4d8cf878" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="8744f14466df4725b526168d4a56ea21"><span data-offset-key="8744f14466df4725b526168d4a56ea21:0">1.1.1 NON-TEXT CONTENT</span></span></span></a><span key="fbf7deea6a4b4410a9b7cdb7a269b852"><span offset-key="fbf7deea6a4b4410a9b7cdb7a269b852:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="dc524391a5984e1d84a6c307387aa786"><span offset-key="dc524391a5984e1d84a6c307387aa786:0">For example, the FedEx logo should have an alt value of "FedEx."</span></span>

<span key="5195b6899e31456a84b50c8d67b9ddc3"><span offset-key="5195b6899e31456a84b50c8d67b9ddc3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#for-images-containing-text-make-sure-the-alt-description-includes-the-images-text" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="64654a6761cc48d2884ae5ba53f6a260" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a4ef8c95884c43369774c9e2a6f340b7"><span data-offset-key="a4ef8c95884c43369774c9e2a6f340b7:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: FOR IMAGES CONTAINING TEXT, MAKE SURE THE ALT DESCRIPTION INCLUDES THE IMAGE'S TEXT.</span></span></span></a><span key="5e09459c1542430690b7b5bcd54acaa0"><span offset-key="5e09459c1542430690b7b5bcd54acaa0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="58da8e9c8dbf403287a07cc257eb9f27"><span offset-key="58da8e9c8dbf403287a07cc257eb9f27:0">Headings</span></span>

<span key="e2000ac3ae4e48d3ad61ebf31c8a9b71"><span offset-key="e2000ac3ae4e48d3ad61ebf31c8a9b71:0">Heading elements (h1, h2, h3, etc.) help break up the content of the page into related "chunks" of information. They are incredibly important for helping people who use assistive technology to understand the meaning of a page or view.</span></span>

<span key="e689be749694412385b14967dd07c625"><span offset-key="e689be749694412385b14967dd07c625:0">Task: Use heading elements to introduce content.</span></span>

<span key="5655495af9c44456b70aa692a954b3e1"><span offset-key="5655495af9c44456b70aa692a954b3e1:0">Use heading elements to introduce content.</span></span>

<span key="f40dd2c2327341f18aeb5007bc93c331"><span offset-key="f40dd2c2327341f18aeb5007bc93c331:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-descriptive.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d755caefd974473994443d23306a512f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="26bc3a933fdd4df083874fa435b77037"><span data-offset-key="26bc3a933fdd4df083874fa435b77037:0">2.4.6 HEADINGS OR LABELS</span></span></span></a><span key="3040dc0686d645fa9712302dd007c2d5"><span offset-key="3040dc0686d645fa9712302dd007c2d5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="bf4dc0c825ae47e88a03000e3abaf218"><span offset-key="bf4dc0c825ae47e88a03000e3abaf218:0">Heading elements construct a document outline, and should not be used for purely visual design.</span></span>

<span key="8eefb2d1477648fc92996c1eb15f4a4f"><span offset-key="8eefb2d1477648fc92996c1eb15f4a4f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-heading-elements-to-introduce-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="737b820de85349809ed15185e546a65f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="41cdf2b6b6e644bf8f36fce851a6b8d4"><span data-offset-key="41cdf2b6b6e644bf8f36fce851a6b8d4:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE HEADING ELEMENTS TO INTRODUCE CONTENT.</span></span></span></a><span key="56f9eed51b084e6dad54d944f6e30aaf"><span offset-key="56f9eed51b084e6dad54d944f6e30aaf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="3d07a28bce8d4bcc9dcae83f3f43a345"><span offset-key="3d07a28bce8d4bcc9dcae83f3f43a345:0">Task: Use only one </span>`h1`<span offset-key="3d07a28bce8d4bcc9dcae83f3f43a345:2"> element per page or view.</span></span>

<span key="1222289a32ce40d28efde5bc7fe88e68"><span offset-key="1222289a32ce40d28efde5bc7fe88e68:0">Use only one </span>`h1`<span offset-key="1222289a32ce40d28efde5bc7fe88e68:2"> element per page or view.</span></span>

<span key="044ff98044fe420995714e2d7b4d6bbd"><span offset-key="044ff98044fe420995714e2d7b4d6bbd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-descriptive.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="40e90d6d7c8b4f72b4cb7ff55c7440c0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="79c84033451c4a488878ccd573765030"><span data-offset-key="79c84033451c4a488878ccd573765030:0">2.4.6 HEADINGS OR LABELS</span></span></span></a><span key="bb3d962d5911479594a2dac2c2d30e77"><span offset-key="bb3d962d5911479594a2dac2c2d30e77:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="cae1aa4d890146608e0a63728f3cc3e8"><span offset-key="cae1aa4d890146608e0a63728f3cc3e8:0">The </span>`h1`<span offset-key="cae1aa4d890146608e0a63728f3cc3e8:2"> element should be used to communicate the high-level purpose of the page or view. Do not use the </span>`h1`<span offset-key="cae1aa4d890146608e0a63728f3cc3e8:4"> element for a heading that does not change between pages or views (for example, the site's name).</span></span>

<span key="b758994b36f141cf958588ed9876c1d8"><span offset-key="b758994b36f141cf958588ed9876c1d8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-only-one-h1-element-per-page-or-view" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="337b734dda5b4576bcc8cc86f4e72ddd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="81ef7c78497e4c9db41b97c0682d916d"><span data-offset-key="81ef7c78497e4c9db41b97c0682d916d:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE ONLY ONE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="81ef7c78497e4c9db41b97c0682d916d:1">H1</code><span data-offset-key="81ef7c78497e4c9db41b97c0682d916d:2"> ELEMENT PER PAGE OR VIEW.</span></span></span></a><span key="9a2c0566a15f458f9b47c707a1b5d636"><span offset-key="9a2c0566a15f458f9b47c707a1b5d636:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a56d88cb5616402f927a58c7b67314a0"><span offset-key="a56d88cb5616402f927a58c7b67314a0:0">Task: Heading elements should be written in a logical sequence.</span></span>

<span key="943463fe519148c4924f47c148063e00"><span offset-key="943463fe519148c4924f47c148063e00:0">Heading elements should be written in a logical sequence.</span></span>

<span key="0cf2737f4bda43da9a55a7ce33f3cdb2"><span offset-key="0cf2737f4bda43da9a55a7ce33f3cdb2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-descriptive.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a3bb1cc026c44e59b84b4f808ecac1f8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="b414df523944489e98f662513d500c7f"><span data-offset-key="b414df523944489e98f662513d500c7f:0">2.4.6 HEADINGS OR LABELS</span></span></span></a><span key="c6a4caf38c2f48cb9d1a9ef8cfc6fdff"><span offset-key="c6a4caf38c2f48cb9d1a9ef8cfc6fdff:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="bfd4da364d0943e8848ec20f4e0f0d6c"><span offset-key="bfd4da364d0943e8848ec20f4e0f0d6c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://webdesign.tutsplus.com/articles/the-importance-of-heading-levels-for-assistive-technology--cms-31753" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8c0c8ed9a8c7402fa2708a0ae15a4dfc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7f1eb1bd41414613bb2425c41c9cd2a4"><span data-offset-key="7f1eb1bd41414613bb2425c41c9cd2a4:0">The order of heading elements</span></span></span></a><span key="091309385b8c4101b47f03064d95a826"><span offset-key="091309385b8c4101b47f03064d95a826:0"> should descend, based on the "depth" of the content. For example, a </span>`h4`<span offset-key="091309385b8c4101b47f03064d95a826:2"> element should not appear on a page before the first </span>`h3`<span offset-key="091309385b8c4101b47f03064d95a826:4"> element declaration. A tool such as </span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/resources/#headingsmap" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c04cc890ca114945b3a0bf1b82f6cee5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a999b94fae26498dbb0c12032113c6f7"><span data-offset-key="a999b94fae26498dbb0c12032113c6f7:0">headingsMap</span></span></span></a><span key="346b861e07dd4e5dbc2f825f78251cf1"><span offset-key="346b861e07dd4e5dbc2f825f78251cf1:0"> can help you evaluate this.</span></span>
