<span key="79a3193b719946b8a3d5acb1ddc626ff"><span offset-key="79a3193b719946b8a3d5acb1ddc626ff:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#heading-elements-should-be-written-in-a-logical-sequence" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb9178fa04404973a4c80f42fb20d037" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="9dd47d5d9def438498f2893043aa6055"><span data-offset-key="9dd47d5d9def438498f2893043aa6055:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: HEADING ELEMENTS SHOULD BE WRITTEN IN A LOGICAL SEQUENCE.</span></span></span></a><span key="d5490cf7182c45bc915ff6b1f8ef9ffd"><span offset-key="d5490cf7182c45bc915ff6b1f8ef9ffd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="143dfeba7ea4415384507b98f35d6c4a"><span offset-key="143dfeba7ea4415384507b98f35d6c4a:0">Task: Don't skip heading levels.</span></span>

<span key="749edfa2b95d4f8db4907e5c8c212d35"><span offset-key="749edfa2b95d4f8db4907e5c8c212d35:0">Don't skip heading levels.</span></span>

<span key="6dca6054f33545b482e93a42a223c0e0"><span offset-key="6dca6054f33545b482e93a42a223c0e0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-descriptive.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="242850b40f2b4e1294346cb7cd16b606" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="4bbfa9c1ff264379b5bb3d0feaa01ce7"><span data-offset-key="4bbfa9c1ff264379b5bb3d0feaa01ce7:0">2.4.6 HEADINGS OR LABELS</span></span></span></a><span key="eb80b58c5d144c41bc4e6ab46e7cc762"><span offset-key="eb80b58c5d144c41bc4e6ab46e7cc762:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="266be02e9dbc4a0c8026964e013d1f65"><span offset-key="266be02e9dbc4a0c8026964e013d1f65:0">For example, don't jump from a </span>`h2`<span offset-key="266be02e9dbc4a0c8026964e013d1f65:2"> to a </span>`h4`<span offset-key="266be02e9dbc4a0c8026964e013d1f65:4">, skipping a </span>`h3`<span offset-key="266be02e9dbc4a0c8026964e013d1f65:6"> element. If heading levels are being skipped for a specific visual treatment, use CSS classes instead.</span></span>

<span key="88d62330e1a34de2a45647575a3199c4"><span offset-key="88d62330e1a34de2a45647575a3199c4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#dont-skip-heading-levels" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="56df3b56de6d4903a22ddc0f1ff303da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="80dcee1bda4f4c70a169d97af40efc37"><span data-offset-key="80dcee1bda4f4c70a169d97af40efc37:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: DON'T SKIP HEADING LEVELS.</span></span></span></a><span key="24d975b053de42f89d38abce41fc485a"><span offset-key="24d975b053de42f89d38abce41fc485a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="4699f1e0606d40aa9a0ac4829e9190cb"><span offset-key="4699f1e0606d40aa9a0ac4829e9190cb:0">Lists</span></span>

<span key="274bd25998b84f358d4c932c98711ad6"><span offset-key="274bd25998b84f358d4c932c98711ad6:0">Lists elements let people know a collection of items are related and if they are sequential, and how many items are present in the list grouping.</span></span>

<span key="ced92361ff5041e0b7388a4aca0579d7"><span offset-key="ced92361ff5041e0b7388a4aca0579d7:0">Task: Use list elements (</span>`ol`<span offset-key="ced92361ff5041e0b7388a4aca0579d7:2">, </span>`ul`<span offset-key="ced92361ff5041e0b7388a4aca0579d7:4">, and </span>`dl`<span offset-key="ced92361ff5041e0b7388a4aca0579d7:6"> elements) for list content.</span></span>

<span key="e7dcf4f170aa40ee8e9fc9ad21245fe2"><span offset-key="e7dcf4f170aa40ee8e9fc9ad21245fe2:0">Use list elements (</span>`ol`<span offset-key="e7dcf4f170aa40ee8e9fc9ad21245fe2:2">, </span>`ul`<span offset-key="e7dcf4f170aa40ee8e9fc9ad21245fe2:4">, and </span>`dl`<span offset-key="e7dcf4f170aa40ee8e9fc9ad21245fe2:6"> elements) for list content.</span></span>

<span key="ffad859a99204ae59bf0b17a5d1fb8cc"><span offset-key="ffad859a99204ae59bf0b17a5d1fb8cc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="04515cc444444c9fa6b369d4b1b7e0ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a97efab0c7574b1eb2de8377f0b37798"><span data-offset-key="a97efab0c7574b1eb2de8377f0b37798:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="371c7f129d794eee887120e303e92361"><span offset-key="371c7f129d794eee887120e303e92361:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="90eda4ff69984e52964a77c79022a71a"><span offset-key="90eda4ff69984e52964a77c79022a71a:0">This may include sections of related content, items visually displayed in a grid-like layout, or sibling a elements.</span></span>

<span key="cf790bdab0c345ec85c0111185fe9699"><span offset-key="cf790bdab0c345ec85c0111185fe9699:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-list-elements-ol-ul-and-dl-elements-for-list-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a9fe40c04b85430395fdf0edadc384b9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f"><span data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE LIST ELEMENTS (</span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:1">OL</code><span data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:2">, </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:3">UL</code><span data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:4">, AND </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:5">DL</code><span data-offset-key="3139c3cdc24f461e827f309625a1cd4f:6"> ELEMENTS) FOR LIST CONTENT.</span></span></span></a><span key="354c004167a34827a9e9164d2aba65c9"><span offset-key="354c004167a34827a9e9164d2aba65c9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="368bded058854642accb7ddb43af8c93"><span offset-key="368bded058854642accb7ddb43af8c93:0">Controls</span></span>

<span key="5b0314b43d3b47a4b7df17266d466254"><span offset-key="5b0314b43d3b47a4b7df17266d466254:0">Controls are interactive elements such as links and buttons that let a person navigate to a destination or perform an action.</span></span>

<span key="723d7eac17f64cf68420ae0c087396fa"><span offset-key="723d7eac17f64cf68420ae0c087396fa:0">Task: Use the </span>`a`<span offset-key="723d7eac17f64cf68420ae0c087396fa:2"> element for links.</span></span>

<span key="652ec81f52a54110811072508fa54060"><span offset-key="652ec81f52a54110811072508fa54060:0">Use the </span>`a`<span offset-key="652ec81f52a54110811072508fa54060:2"> element for links.</span></span>

<span key="2e8300fe527540cd8d7346057eac68e3"><span offset-key="2e8300fe527540cd8d7346057eac68e3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a9ac0f6e9cdd4e2d920df64f717fc497" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="2181d46fa0f048bdbd9ce072c65ef887"><span data-offset-key="2181d46fa0f048bdbd9ce072c65ef887:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="711028040c424b2d8cf192b57d706e09"><span offset-key="711028040c424b2d8cf192b57d706e09:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406"><span offset-key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406:0">Links should always have a </span>`href`<span offset-key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406:2"> attribute, even when used in Single Page Applications (SPAs). Without a </span>`href`<span offset-key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406:4"> attribute, the link will not be properly exposed to assistive technology. An example of this would be a link that uses an </span>`onclick`<span offset-key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406:6"> event, in place of a </span>`href`<span offset-key="4a65064b3f184461a2565eace7514406:8"> attribute.</span></span>

<span key="27fc5d2571be40c6b7975376a98a7278"><span offset-key="27fc5d2571be40c6b7975376a98a7278:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-the-a-element-for-links" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f26b603885714da29e6520e1c9ef3887" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="deb4ba59284349589499e0d441a67364"><span data-offset-key="deb4ba59284349589499e0d441a67364:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="deb4ba59284349589499e0d441a67364:1">A</code><span data-offset-key="deb4ba59284349589499e0d441a67364:2"> ELEMENT FOR LINKS.</span></span></span></a><span key="17db9347114e46d4b5025fb0013eefb7"><span offset-key="17db9347114e46d4b5025fb0013eefb7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b4f78cb049654e0fa7702ec6b7eab8ec"><span offset-key="b4f78cb049654e0fa7702ec6b7eab8ec:0">Task: Ensure that links are recognizable as links.</span></span>

<span key="d8c980717a9f4c328ac172015f3c4a40"><span offset-key="d8c980717a9f4c328ac172015f3c4a40:0">Ensure that links are recognizable as links.</span></span>

<span key="a62abbd2df1a429882563188888fd0a5"><span offset-key="a62abbd2df1a429882563188888fd0a5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-without-color.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8e437e5a5fb740e890d5c660414efd5e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ed5d84ec532446e6b01f64ea5c9b09ba"><span data-offset-key="ed5d84ec532446e6b01f64ea5c9b09ba:0">1.4.1 USE OF COLOR</span></span></span></a><span key="a389cbb7d2b543e4bb462f2396f29cd5"><span offset-key="a389cbb7d2b543e4bb462f2396f29cd5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="cb534e53ee3f4737bfbfa7d649355095"><span offset-key="cb534e53ee3f4737bfbfa7d649355095:0">Color alone is not sufficient to indicate the presence of a link. Underlines are a popular and commonly-understood way to communicate the presence of link content.</span></span>

<span key="40d8024e90ab40e6992900beffee604b"><span offset-key="40d8024e90ab40e6992900beffee604b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-that-links-are-recognizable-as-links" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5c09f593c0e24754b3fdd7cb89362444" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="1949cfaf412b401299d0f28b201d8fcd"><span data-offset-key="1949cfaf412b401299d0f28b201d8fcd:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE THAT LINKS ARE RECOGNIZABLE AS LINKS.</span></span></span></a><span key="241cc791737e4d1ba27a6951df92e06f"><span offset-key="241cc791737e4d1ba27a6951df92e06f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="ac11c48ce9374408bb3b33a44c72787b"><span offset-key="ac11c48ce9374408bb3b33a44c72787b:0">Task: Ensure that controls have </span>`:focus`<span offset-key="ac11c48ce9374408bb3b33a44c72787b:2"> states.</span></span>

<span key="cf9bc47b71654847af9a0cdce0a48b11"><span offset-key="cf9bc47b71654847af9a0cdce0a48b11:0">Ensure that controls have </span>`:focus`<span offset-key="cf9bc47b71654847af9a0cdce0a48b11:2"> states.</span></span>

<span key="711869f22cc5425ea943e3185a1ddd1f"><span offset-key="711869f22cc5425ea943e3185a1ddd1f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-focus-visible.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="95a4a10bfd2c43ed8c4c84edead72a5b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="5c784ee06b6d4c0e83ccf4c16b07701e"><span data-offset-key="5c784ee06b6d4c0e83ccf4c16b07701e:0">2.4.7 FOCUS VISIBLE</span></span></span></a><span key="925541a2b2b24194b91f02c10071ff03"><span offset-key="925541a2b2b24194b91f02c10071ff03:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="47b475e904b64b70b47679a79079e9de"><span offset-key="47b475e904b64b70b47679a79079e9de:0">Visible focus styles help people determine which interactive element has keyboard focus. This lets them know that they can perform actions like activating a button or navigating to a link's destination.</span></span>

<span key="6671b66a8b6e4163a2ded996c94dd796"><span offset-key="6671b66a8b6e4163a2ded996c94dd796:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-that-controls-have-focus-states" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2a3d0947045949f3afeea0fc082e9aaa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="bf681242570649738eda3d1d9d07b33b"><span data-offset-key="bf681242570649738eda3d1d9d07b33b:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE THAT CONTROLS HAVE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="bf681242570649738eda3d1d9d07b33b:1">:FOCUS</code><span data-offset-key="bf681242570649738eda3d1d9d07b33b:2"> STATES.</span></span></span></a><span key="75edd01bca554a61b85914e463fa3afb"><span offset-key="75edd01bca554a61b85914e463fa3afb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8f33da72c7c045f88a3ffbe8a4fafd2b"><span offset-key="8f33da72c7c045f88a3ffbe8a4fafd2b:0">Task: Use the </span>`button`<span offset-key="8f33da72c7c045f88a3ffbe8a4fafd2b:2"> element for buttons.</span></span>

<span key="b30c37270f5948b7b7de5f2874ee9323"><span offset-key="b30c37270f5948b7b7de5f2874ee9323:0">Use the </span>`button`<span offset-key="b30c37270f5948b7b7de5f2874ee9323:2"> element for buttons.</span></span>

<span key="b31b88075ed74279a2e6c153d47ab588"><span offset-key="b31b88075ed74279a2e6c153d47ab588:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7ce6efff2b1549ab922b45c281b3f1aa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3ab327c20e4346b2858aa5fabd115749"><span data-offset-key="3ab327c20e4346b2858aa5fabd115749:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="fa9862ef3d6142f59f272079141d59d0"><span offset-key="fa9862ef3d6142f59f272079141d59d0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8422e226c87b4ff7a1c47b8148e564f4"><span offset-key="8422e226c87b4ff7a1c47b8148e564f4:0">Buttons are used to submit data or perform an on-screen action which does not shift keyboard focus. You can add </span>`type="button"`<span offset-key="8422e226c87b4ff7a1c47b8148e564f4:2"> to a </span>`button`<span offset-key="8422e226c87b4ff7a1c47b8148e564f4:4"> element to prevent the browser from attempting to submit form information when activated.</span></span>

<span key="0f4f82c03897479b8602722af4b372fb"><span offset-key="0f4f82c03897479b8602722af4b372fb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-the-button-element-for-buttons" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f6742246d9d24125b3762b00ffc3269d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="458e847692a54de79dfdf27ff5c5624b"><span data-offset-key="458e847692a54de79dfdf27ff5c5624b:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="458e847692a54de79dfdf27ff5c5624b:1">BUTTON</code><span data-offset-key="458e847692a54de79dfdf27ff5c5624b:2"> ELEMENT FOR BUTTONS.</span></span></span></a><span key="448fd6b3d3bc49b9899929b85e93ee58"><span offset-key="448fd6b3d3bc49b9899929b85e93ee58:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b17dfed9237a4f1b97def0d9b2050383"><span offset-key="b17dfed9237a4f1b97def0d9b2050383:0">Task: Provide a skip link and make sure that it is visible when focused.</span></span>

<span key="b23fba2377e6425ca3f2fca454c478ed"><span offset-key="b23fba2377e6425ca3f2fca454c478ed:0">Provide a skip link and make sure that it is visible when focused.</span></span>

<span key="6153aae9a2fd4aaeaeb958ca2dc38600"><span offset-key="6153aae9a2fd4aaeaeb958ca2dc38600:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-skip.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a4c0e3a1f0bc46988f96cb5b0e0d9fe4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="add2afe49b664e2dbe4cedd4b515320a"><span data-offset-key="add2afe49b664e2dbe4cedd4b515320a:0">2.4.1 BYPASS BLOCKS</span></span></span></a><span key="9a07c630e1654c849200879d85e2160a"><span offset-key="9a07c630e1654c849200879d85e2160a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="9aedaa07a19d4df7b73838e28e3cbd9f"><span offset-key="9aedaa07a19d4df7b73838e28e3cbd9f:0">A </span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/posts/2013-05-11-skip-nav-links/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c71dd29b8ca0467a9c796bd142dd3282" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3eb04e26ab4946178e0ec0aa5781e7ff"><span data-offset-key="3eb04e26ab4946178e0ec0aa5781e7ff:0">skip link</span></span></span></a><span key="1173a11f66e44e9a9769b62875f0f1d4"><span offset-key="1173a11f66e44e9a9769b62875f0f1d4:0"> can be used to provide quick access to the main content of a page or view. This allows a person to easily bypass globally repeated content such as a website's primary navigation, or persistent search widget.</span></span>

<span key="ddd1435944aa4af0af16abf659692d2b"><span offset-key="ddd1435944aa4af0af16abf659692d2b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#provide-a-skip-link-and-make-sure-that-it-is-visible-when-focused" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d7194fec990c4f69a559ec48cb9f1b74" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="5722890ba6f84e58b8fb008f45f863cf"><span data-offset-key="5722890ba6f84e58b8fb008f45f863cf:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: PROVIDE A SKIP LINK AND MAKE SURE THAT IT IS VISIBLE WHEN FOCUSED.</span></span></span></a><span key="2198b7abe293493d9705df9deea8f7c5"><span offset-key="2198b7abe293493d9705df9deea8f7c5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="405abcbbb6c94b0a85299f5030b6858b"><span offset-key="405abcbbb6c94b0a85299f5030b6858b:0">Task: Identify links that open in a new tab or window.</span></span>

<span key="3e2c6334263c4016b9d2c89f72982622"><span offset-key="3e2c6334263c4016b9d2c89f72982622:0">Identify links that open in a new tab or window.</span></span>

<span key="d33e5719662a4a1a91a1799aec932d93"><span offset-key="d33e5719662a4a1a91a1799aec932d93:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/WCAG20-TECHS/G201.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8520fde953bf4d968a4bf43097a0bfe5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0dda1dbf50c74de2909739db3d286c13"><span data-offset-key="0dda1dbf50c74de2909739db3d286c13:0">G201: GIVING USERS ADVANCED WARNING WHEN OPENING A NEW WINDOW</span></span></span></a><span key="a689629a8ba149db8d0d881102c307cd"><span offset-key="a689629a8ba149db8d0d881102c307cd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f28de2c293d74d1bb042175bfbc78cdf"><span offset-key="f28de2c293d74d1bb042175bfbc78cdf:0">Ideally, avoid links that open in a new tab or window. If a link does, ensure the link's behavior will be communicated in a way that is apparent to all users. Doing this will help people understand what will happen before activating the link. While this technique is technically not required for compliance, it is an often-cited area of frustration for many different kinds of assistive technology users.</span></span>

<span key="8ae17a3dc1e646f48e35c5058914619c"><span offset-key="8ae17a3dc1e646f48e35c5058914619c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#identify-links-that-open-in-a-new-tab-or-window" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="32509e5ac8194cb5bb2779d82b49182e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="f21beeb1ee52436ab2d2b7ace6589156"><span data-offset-key="f21beeb1ee52436ab2d2b7ace6589156:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: IDENTIFY LINKS THAT OPEN IN A NEW TAB OR WINDOW.</span></span></span></a><span key="e996ed807495440ebe5216695e1d6338"><span offset-key="e996ed807495440ebe5216695e1d6338:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="d25ea6548ee7453b8c066d7f56709dbd"><span offset-key="d25ea6548ee7453b8c066d7f56709dbd:0">Tables</span></span>

<span key="1035ac286636480c91db6b0ce9af5676"><span offset-key="1035ac286636480c91db6b0ce9af5676:0">Tables are a structured set of data that help people understand the relationships between different types of information.</span></span>

<span key="a902685efbb04ceead58cb251cd797f9"><span offset-key="a902685efbb04ceead58cb251cd797f9:0">Task: Use the </span>`table`<span offset-key="a902685efbb04ceead58cb251cd797f9:2"> element to describe tabular data.</span></span>

<span key="379ac6a8990c455d95830e7ceb419055"><span offset-key="379ac6a8990c455d95830e7ceb419055:0">Use the </span>`table`<span offset-key="379ac6a8990c455d95830e7ceb419055:2"> element to describe tabular data.</span></span>

<span key="12efaa1def754129a93a68d532034e5e"><span offset-key="12efaa1def754129a93a68d532034e5e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b3604421cd7148ea8fff891fc5e862a4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ea7515401b88439180c2ec46b9aa8d32"><span data-offset-key="ea7515401b88439180c2ec46b9aa8d32:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="7909c2f85e844cb298292e1dfcd7ea68"><span offset-key="7909c2f85e844cb298292e1dfcd7ea68:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="556f664e6b5a447f87d352c6ab97b101"><span offset-key="556f664e6b5a447f87d352c6ab97b101:0">Do you need to display data in rows and columns? Use the </span>`table`<span offset-key="556f664e6b5a447f87d352c6ab97b101:2"> element.</span></span>

<span key="ea365a1d29134b059492cc5e751e482d"><span offset-key="ea365a1d29134b059492cc5e751e482d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-the-table-element-to-describe-tabular-data" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e8bd5e610dfc4a01bc1baf79a01f9655" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="83c4723e63fd4185bd1fd12fe4265761"><span data-offset-key="83c4723e63fd4185bd1fd12fe4265761:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="83c4723e63fd4185bd1fd12fe4265761:1">TABLE</code><span data-offset-key="83c4723e63fd4185bd1fd12fe4265761:2"> ELEMENT TO DESCRIBE TABULAR DATA.</span></span></span></a><span key="e00f58e0c6fa42d988107718b512ad26"><span offset-key="e00f58e0c6fa42d988107718b512ad26:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="eb3efb6ad56f4652832a81094bb41dae"><span offset-key="eb3efb6ad56f4652832a81094bb41dae:0">Task: Use the </span>`th`<span offset-key="eb3efb6ad56f4652832a81094bb41dae:2"> element for table headers (with appropriate </span>`scope`<span offset-key="eb3efb6ad56f4652832a81094bb41dae:4"> attributes).</span></span>

<span key="366ea85bf3a74ab891c0b240554ce336"><span offset-key="366ea85bf3a74ab891c0b240554ce336:0">Use the </span>`th`<span offset-key="366ea85bf3a74ab891c0b240554ce336:2"> element for table headers (with appropriate </span>`scope`<span offset-key="366ea85bf3a74ab891c0b240554ce336:4"> attributes).</span></span>

<span key="0fbf2bc0399c48f797f5eb44647ab4f3"><span offset-key="0fbf2bc0399c48f797f5eb44647ab4f3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/ensure-compat-parses.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd1f042bfedf4f43a28242494fe87348" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="03c6da94700849ebab4326592335809f"><span data-offset-key="03c6da94700849ebab4326592335809f:0">4.1.1 PARSING</span></span></span></a><span key="700556e8aed6459cbae74f7602fa9c02"><span offset-key="700556e8aed6459cbae74f7602fa9c02:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a0051de43f0c441c900cd5a772d654ea"><span offset-key="a0051de43f0c441c900cd5a772d654ea:0">Depending on </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/tutorials/tables/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ee7feb6d9bcd4483bc4fc4d6b23262d1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="17af462f007748798f01256f9da8bc2b"><span data-offset-key="17af462f007748798f01256f9da8bc2b:0">how complex your table is</span></span></span></a><span key="f186d338d7b141dbb42232e35848bc57"><span offset-key="f186d338d7b141dbb42232e35848bc57:0">, you may also consider using </span>`scope="col"`<span offset-key="f186d338d7b141dbb42232e35848bc57:2"> for column headers, and </span>`scope="row"`<span offset-key="f186d338d7b141dbb42232e35848bc57:4"> for row headers. Many different kinds of assistive technology still use the </span>`scope`<span offset-key="f186d338d7b141dbb42232e35848bc57:6"> attribute to help them understand and describe the structure of a table.</span></span>

<span key="f68ab2f43cde4238b6b47a3982ea9d40"><span offset-key="f68ab2f43cde4238b6b47a3982ea9d40:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-the-th-element-for-table-headers-with-appropriate-scope-attributes" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="32a7ec91cf0641d789352b39ebbff88b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded"><span data-offset-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded:1">TH</code><span data-offset-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded:2"> ELEMENT FOR TABLE HEADERS (WITH APPROPRIATE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded:3">SCOPE</code><span data-offset-key="88d0e250505449a7a51b6bdfa7cfdded:4"> ATTRIBUTES).</span></span></span></a><span key="4b0d3abd03b74756adaa113919d853be"><span offset-key="4b0d3abd03b74756adaa113919d853be:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="73605ec5f18b404b8407e9fdef8d92e2"><span offset-key="73605ec5f18b404b8407e9fdef8d92e2:0">Task: Use the </span>`caption`<span offset-key="73605ec5f18b404b8407e9fdef8d92e2:2"> element to provide a title for the table.</span></span>

<span key="5fab01e75d664ef28c4cf9f2cb6b7e73"><span offset-key="5fab01e75d664ef28c4cf9f2cb6b7e73:0">Use the </span>`caption`<span offset-key="5fab01e75d664ef28c4cf9f2cb6b7e73:2"> element to provide a title for the table.</span></span>

<span key="e04bee6a418d4737853a75aebc0dcab1"><span offset-key="e04bee6a418d4737853a75aebc0dcab1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-descriptive.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6fa63b25aec84d8e870522d943632c82" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="461dec9860b84ca38568955e47eb24da"><span data-offset-key="461dec9860b84ca38568955e47eb24da:0">2.4.6 HEADINGS OR LABELS</span></span></span></a><span key="5467a23897704932b12a39100b525ca0"><span offset-key="5467a23897704932b12a39100b525ca0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="0fc9b751aa0d498ab3ce90417b65822e"><span offset-key="0fc9b751aa0d498ab3ce90417b65822e:0">The table's </span>`caption`<span offset-key="0fc9b751aa0d498ab3ce90417b65822e:2"> should describe what kind of information the table contains.</span></span>

<span key="da53963a545a4d9e9885461e57fc4a18"><span offset-key="da53963a545a4d9e9885461e57fc4a18:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-the-caption-element-to-provide-a-title-for-the-table" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d57b251462ef4a56bf02b7bdcfd86b2f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="e48b8db324f949969cc8efa8f267de30"><span data-offset-key="e48b8db324f949969cc8efa8f267de30:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="e48b8db324f949969cc8efa8f267de30:1">CAPTION</code><span data-offset-key="e48b8db324f949969cc8efa8f267de30:2"> ELEMENT TO PROVIDE A TITLE FOR THE TABLE.</span></span></span></a><span key="65dd19ea64ac4adb93511686cf609071"><span offset-key="65dd19ea64ac4adb93511686cf609071:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="30f4d762f3f4468a83598d84b0758516"><span offset-key="30f4d762f3f4468a83598d84b0758516:0">Forms</span></span>

<span key="5a12dfe885f24205b8913cc1a4851fb2"><span offset-key="5a12dfe885f24205b8913cc1a4851fb2:0">Forms allow people to enter information into a site for processing and manipulation. This includes things like sending messages and placing orders.</span></span>

<span key="21be935c5c5e47fbaaf41475ef9c2dc0"><span offset-key="21be935c5c5e47fbaaf41475ef9c2dc0:0">Task: All inputs in a form are associated with a corresponding </span>`label`<span offset-key="21be935c5c5e47fbaaf41475ef9c2dc0:2"> element.</span></span>

<span key="2a38de14d560451e9947bd69c05654e4"><span offset-key="2a38de14d560451e9947bd69c05654e4:0">All inputs in a form are associated with a corresponding </span>`label`<span offset-key="2a38de14d560451e9947bd69c05654e4:2"> element.</span></span>

<span key="17bbcb5499f94a86b2b875aca84c697a"><span offset-key="17bbcb5499f94a86b2b875aca84c697a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/consistent-behavior-unpredictable-change.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0a9f555a4a554cdf902030e2a9d9568a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="04b178a542ec4aa785006e9a555ea98a"><span data-offset-key="04b178a542ec4aa785006e9a555ea98a:0">3.2.2 ON INPUT</span></span></span></a><span key="10189c9f2b8d40a19acaecdc2b3abf1d"><span offset-key="10189c9f2b8d40a19acaecdc2b3abf1d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="06b28f9a0cbc413ba50b8f001897be93"><span offset-key="06b28f9a0cbc413ba50b8f001897be93:0">Use a </span>`for`<span offset-key="06b28f9a0cbc413ba50b8f001897be93:2">/</span>`id`<span offset-key="06b28f9a0cbc413ba50b8f001897be93:4"> pairing to guarantee the highest level of browser/assistive technology support.</span></span>

<span key="7237ba7afdec4a0c92f395ef6cb0b87e"><span offset-key="7237ba7afdec4a0c92f395ef6cb0b87e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#all-inputs-in-a-form-are-associated-with-a-corresponding-label-element" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="93c89bb3e4834d12a0aad975e7ce7d40" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="9b409097155e4693b0492606722aca4d"><span data-offset-key="9b409097155e4693b0492606722aca4d:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ALL INPUTS IN A FORM ARE ASSOCIATED WITH A CORRESPONDING </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="9b409097155e4693b0492606722aca4d:1">LABEL</code><span data-offset-key="9b409097155e4693b0492606722aca4d:2"> ELEMENT.</span></span></span></a><span key="f42c6a0006bf4deb932f5b8809242cea"><span offset-key="f42c6a0006bf4deb932f5b8809242cea:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="d7da44e3ea7d4adca2b55fcd080c94e2"><span offset-key="d7da44e3ea7d4adca2b55fcd080c94e2:0">Task: Use </span>`fieldset`<span offset-key="d7da44e3ea7d4adca2b55fcd080c94e2:2"> and </span>`legend`<span offset-key="d7da44e3ea7d4adca2b55fcd080c94e2:4"> elements where appropriate.</span></span>

<span key="8b51b1a961f945fda2727c4ff3564768"><span offset-key="8b51b1a961f945fda2727c4ff3564768:0">Use </span>`fieldset`<span offset-key="8b51b1a961f945fda2727c4ff3564768:2"> and </span>`legend`<span offset-key="8b51b1a961f945fda2727c4ff3564768:4"> elements where appropriate.</span></span>

<span key="3ed7eeac6c4e48498dde78d3fd0da6af"><span offset-key="3ed7eeac6c4e48498dde78d3fd0da6af:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e64bcc25aae64f6f9d07a408d39f2a28" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="79dc92edb7f34216a0abfc8c51788bcb"><span data-offset-key="79dc92edb7f34216a0abfc8c51788bcb:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="f418148f8b50409a94ab19821fe8318d"><span offset-key="f418148f8b50409a94ab19821fe8318d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5a967d7d3fe54e74a8771e936ec654a0"><span offset-key="5a967d7d3fe54e74a8771e936ec654a0:0">Does your form contain multiple sections of related inputs? Use </span>`fieldset`<span offset-key="5a967d7d3fe54e74a8771e936ec654a0:2"> to group them, and </span>`legend`<span offset-key="5a967d7d3fe54e74a8771e936ec654a0:4"> to provide a label for what this section is for.</span></span>

<span key="3aa96cefff0f48be99eac217f761e0c5"><span offset-key="3aa96cefff0f48be99eac217f761e0c5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-fieldset-and-legend-elements-where-appropriate" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="18fd5362cd4540b5bd5f2dd88e4f724d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4"><span data-offset-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4:1">FIELDSET</code><span data-offset-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4:2"> AND </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4:3">LEGEND</code><span data-offset-key="cfe11e7029704ad2910f2f7befd85ca4:4"> ELEMENTS WHERE APPROPRIATE.</span></span></span></a><span key="392e9c318b364e648e283d376ecd9e21"><span offset-key="392e9c318b364e648e283d376ecd9e21:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="0a078558ae9f4f07a46bbd5d838ec83c"><span offset-key="0a078558ae9f4f07a46bbd5d838ec83c:0">Task: Inputs use </span>`autocomplete`<span offset-key="0a078558ae9f4f07a46bbd5d838ec83c:2"> where appropriate.</span></span>

<span key="834928b13a0e4606ad157d4f030cdd2c"><span offset-key="834928b13a0e4606ad157d4f030cdd2c:0">Inputs use </span>`autocomplete`<span offset-key="834928b13a0e4606ad157d4f030cdd2c:2"> where appropriate.</span></span>

<span key="1f20574f599b4d0f905718232173d6e1"><span offset-key="1f20574f599b4d0f905718232173d6e1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/identify-input-purpose.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c6541fb1d619470ba0c3c483945be020" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="66fc50b19acc456c8438f957ec64b262"><span data-offset-key="66fc50b19acc456c8438f957ec64b262:0">1.3.5 IDENTIFY INPUT PURPOSE</span></span></span></a><span key="4efb3acd554c432cb17a832e74868282"><span offset-key="4efb3acd554c432cb17a832e74868282:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="7d197e58a0ad47e9b4e86699ec7ba303"><span offset-key="7d197e58a0ad47e9b4e86699ec7ba303:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/html52/sec-forms.html#sec-autofill" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e3a268a1d6c94f2d945cf09f4d508890" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="fc2b9f0724c14525936bf46c678b790e"><span data-offset-key="fc2b9f0724c14525936bf46c678b790e:0">Providing a mechanism</span></span></span></a><span key="83c12b4c9e2243729aa986fb0444bab7"><span offset-key="83c12b4c9e2243729aa986fb0444bab7:0"> to help people more quickly, easily, and accurately fill in form fields that ask for common information (for example, name, address, phone number).</span></span>

<span key="5164d4666b4f43e1a381735b4de4bd20"><span offset-key="5164d4666b4f43e1a381735b4de4bd20:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#inputs-use-autocomplete-where-appropriate" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="63d1d0d6023442eda2d386402f7c7e77" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0249dfd81d324fbb88279e722b41e633"><span data-offset-key="0249dfd81d324fbb88279e722b41e633:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: INPUTS USE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="0249dfd81d324fbb88279e722b41e633:1">AUTOCOMPLETE</code><span data-offset-key="0249dfd81d324fbb88279e722b41e633:2"> WHERE APPROPRIATE.</span></span></span></a><span key="ed527e9956ca4e9f9ea6b18ba18c2180"><span offset-key="ed527e9956ca4e9f9ea6b18ba18c2180:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="fb50de546a504bda93d43f026d232b83"><span offset-key="fb50de546a504bda93d43f026d232b83:0">Task: Make sure that form input errors are displayed in list above the form after submission.</span></span>

<span key="699c72b3f6f847c787ac55e4731beb5a"><span offset-key="699c72b3f6f847c787ac55e4731beb5a:0">Make sure that form input errors are displayed in list above the form after submission.</span></span>

<span key="175119f0e2984e9fa9f3a1a54c8a816d"><span offset-key="175119f0e2984e9fa9f3a1a54c8a816d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/minimize-error-identified.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dc5b65c1793044abb8371434a18e3b19" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="623c49c5b0bb4f208f4c2fa3009a59f9"><span data-offset-key="623c49c5b0bb4f208f4c2fa3009a59f9:0">3.3.1 ERROR IDENTIFICATION</span></span></span></a><span key="ec8f54ad37a9406cbc7276f332cbd0cd"><span offset-key="ec8f54ad37a9406cbc7276f332cbd0cd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="9fc12fe101e44deea0a53ac7d25ea28b"><span offset-key="9fc12fe101e44deea0a53ac7d25ea28b:0">This provides a way for assistive technology users to quickly have a high-level understanding of what issues are present in the form. This is especially important for larger forms with many inputs. Make sure that each reported error also has a link to the corresponding field with invalid input.</span></span>

<span key="a678b0e0ed9442b1bd3fd8e51795a9f8"><span offset-key="a678b0e0ed9442b1bd3fd8e51795a9f8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-form-input-errors-are-displayed-in-list-above-the-form-after-submission" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f649c6ed501478d9a5acc7d54fdd76f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="334c24454d7442349f52d2ba16262847"><span data-offset-key="334c24454d7442349f52d2ba16262847:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT FORM INPUT ERRORS ARE DISPLAYED IN LIST ABOVE THE FORM AFTER SUBMISSION.</span></span></span></a><span key="9f86a7c9a9bf481b9503b1db10408c63"><span offset-key="9f86a7c9a9bf481b9503b1db10408c63:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="9a0d21fe0bda4d05bc30c74d46f4c7e5"><span offset-key="9a0d21fe0bda4d05bc30c74d46f4c7e5:0">Task: Associate input error messaging with the input it corresponds to.</span></span>

<span key="e436837e3e9446e4b5f884eaa8e8abe3"><span offset-key="e436837e3e9446e4b5f884eaa8e8abe3:0">Associate input error messaging with the input it corresponds to.</span></span>

<span key="9ce4f6f112ac4c39b1c85a97805b46ad"><span offset-key="9ce4f6f112ac4c39b1c85a97805b46ad:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/minimize-error-identified.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="eb023ddba1ad4a6082c0732a58e41e1b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="f29484c26c4d45e09ec9c5a565e714a6"><span data-offset-key="f29484c26c4d45e09ec9c5a565e714a6:0">3.3.1 ERROR IDENTIFICATION</span></span></span></a><span key="98bc81209a8841628db097d4aff39307"><span offset-key="98bc81209a8841628db097d4aff39307:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="4b7529fa4cec44b1a9b034d5fce5629f"><span offset-key="4b7529fa4cec44b1a9b034d5fce5629f:0">Techniques such as </span></span><a href="https://developer.paciellogroup.com/blog/2018/09/describing-aria-describedby/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8aa9d60d6350462c8fa46492168b9a92" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3b69972b3718460ead505056840498d6"><span data-offset-key="3b69972b3718460ead505056840498d6:0">using </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3b69972b3718460ead505056840498d6:1">aria-describedby</code></span></span></a><span key="bd1ae701f43d45578849355b6ad93cda"><span offset-key="bd1ae701f43d45578849355b6ad93cda:0"> allow people who use assistive technology to more easily understand the difference between the input and the error message associated with it.</span></span>

<span key="6876f490b41b44f8906fba4ec3a8f774"><span offset-key="6876f490b41b44f8906fba4ec3a8f774:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#associate-input-error-messaging-with-the-input-it-corresponds-to" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="393c94e02bda400b93c1fa0c5e521709" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="14db3961d7764805acb7cf750d5906fb"><span data-offset-key="14db3961d7764805acb7cf750d5906fb:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ASSOCIATE INPUT ERROR MESSAGING WITH THE INPUT IT CORRESPONDS TO.</span></span></span></a><span key="c1af71b3a9e34ca18f73cb6cfdf9fd85"><span offset-key="c1af71b3a9e34ca18f73cb6cfdf9fd85:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="95ec4a9a002b40048fb09cecfb26d86c"><span offset-key="95ec4a9a002b40048fb09cecfb26d86c:0">Task: Make sure that error, warning, and success states are not visually communicated by just color.</span></span>

<span key="ea6d334c0e2449c4b632e4bec1df9020"><span offset-key="ea6d334c0e2449c4b632e4bec1df9020:0">Make sure that error, warning, and success states are not visually communicated by just color.</span></span>

<span key="65e28cf2cd4c4fe5aec550b96fcb38f7"><span offset-key="65e28cf2cd4c4fe5aec550b96fcb38f7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-without-color.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a000f8c30706410494b2703f8820674d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7e7705465e9d4c3ea225246d1ef7eb60"><span data-offset-key="7e7705465e9d4c3ea225246d1ef7eb60:0">1.4.1 USE OF COLOR</span></span></span></a><span key="275bffd1bae340a9aaede9bce4c7e0af"><span offset-key="275bffd1bae340a9aaede9bce4c7e0af:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a090b8aff5b8401e933ecfd89791fc00"><span offset-key="a090b8aff5b8401e933ecfd89791fc00:0">People who are color blind, who have other low vision conditions, or different cultural understandings for color may not see the state change, or understand what kind of feedback the state represents if color is the only indicator.</span></span>

<span key="e8e705e7419943a0976335784b5322b0"><span offset-key="e8e705e7419943a0976335784b5322b0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-error-warning-and-success-states-are-not-visually-communicated-by-just-color" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bbecb08ad2a8488e9730ed0afc4ed544" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7d03581da55641c29c6b87bae1744e8d"><span data-offset-key="7d03581da55641c29c6b87bae1744e8d:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT ERROR, WARNING, AND SUCCESS STATES ARE NOT VISUALLY COMMUNICATED BY JUST COLOR.</span></span></span></a><span key="f18e30b4dd894622ab96781d0d017079"><span offset-key="f18e30b4dd894622ab96781d0d017079:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="9c1fc94089c1469cbb5ddb900afcfa95"><span offset-key="9c1fc94089c1469cbb5ddb900afcfa95:0">Media</span></span>

<span key="26eed26f094641b48ad12b52baf75c43"><span offset-key="26eed26f094641b48ad12b52baf75c43:0">Media includes content such as pre-recorded and live audio and video.</span></span>

<span key="92fd1018953d4c49b7d9d9773a3e44d9"><span offset-key="92fd1018953d4c49b7d9d9773a3e44d9:0">Task: Make sure that media does not autoplay.</span></span>

<span key="2eb532907d2045f595a1b37a759fa88a"><span offset-key="2eb532907d2045f595a1b37a759fa88a:0">Make sure that media does not autoplay.</span></span>

<span key="6b5ca1df60894404b331405183588421"><span offset-key="6b5ca1df60894404b331405183588421:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-dis-audio.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="479812801b4a4e55b0b528bc63e5e53f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="747f6b31062449048d3ba3b2a865222a"><span data-offset-key="747f6b31062449048d3ba3b2a865222a:0">1.4.2 AUDIO CONTROL</span></span></span></a><span key="d9836b8f73c84710957f4734fad5fb72"><span offset-key="d9836b8f73c84710957f4734fad5fb72:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="c80435d7147e45d0afd88c56736d7b55"><span offset-key="c80435d7147e45d0afd88c56736d7b55:0">Unexpected video and audio can be distracting and disruptive, especially for certain kinds of cognitive disability such as ADHD. Certain kinds of autoplaying video and animation can be a trigger for vestibular and seizure disorders.</span></span>

<span key="040e8489614b467b97350898795659f7"><span offset-key="040e8489614b467b97350898795659f7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-that-media-does-not-autoplay" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ace49ec3f4a540b086304f452a88ab44" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ad36b7ecad2f4c04854fcc94645b016d"><span data-offset-key="ad36b7ecad2f4c04854fcc94645b016d:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE THAT MEDIA DOES NOT AUTOPLAY.</span></span></span></a><span key="0da0bc7258cc488986460bb37f897f99"><span offset-key="0da0bc7258cc488986460bb37f897f99:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="4518629dd67c4abea32c3ffabfb45d27"><span offset-key="4518629dd67c4abea32c3ffabfb45d27:0">Task: Ensure that media controls use appropriate markup.</span></span>

<span key="1a64ad47fc2345978025bcbc04049419"><span offset-key="1a64ad47fc2345978025bcbc04049419:0">Ensure that media controls use appropriate markup.</span></span>

<span key="d43f8cd822084a858827301a877ee60a"><span offset-key="d43f8cd822084a858827301a877ee60a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-programmatic.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="742399673cf74e8fb2138653f7ed172c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="e417bfe6bbc7407ca2f0b6168671b9d1"><span data-offset-key="e417bfe6bbc7407ca2f0b6168671b9d1:0">1.3.1 INFO AND RELATIONSHIPS</span></span></span></a><span key="5e7bc257581d400f8907a82f7a0ad38e"><span offset-key="5e7bc257581d400f8907a82f7a0ad38e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="1b34e26dbead49fbb36161af854de449"><span offset-key="1b34e26dbead49fbb36161af854de449:0">Examples include making sure an audio mute button has </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/PF/aria/states_and_properties#aria-pressed" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7cec58878a044411b5516865219d8cff" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="9c9794ed1f994dcbbd733d65e9fe4262"><span data-offset-key="9c9794ed1f994dcbbd733d65e9fe4262:0">a pressed toggle state</span></span></span></a><span key="7de326b8a96b423a8da94c35832678d1"><span offset-key="7de326b8a96b423a8da94c35832678d1:0"> when active, or that a volume slider uses </span>`<input type="range">`<span offset-key="7de326b8a96b423a8da94c35832678d1:2">.</span></span>

<span key="e883906c86b24e1a9aca19b3acfd8648"><span offset-key="e883906c86b24e1a9aca19b3acfd8648:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-that-media-controls-use-appropriate-markup" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b063254bf06a4b4a8c84d6e4f53d2da1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d37dff0303f44bd5aa21005cfdd7f38f"><span data-offset-key="d37dff0303f44bd5aa21005cfdd7f38f:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE THAT MEDIA CONTROLS USE APPROPRIATE MARKUP.</span></span></span></a><span key="3590ea0729414a78b237563ed2158abc"><span offset-key="3590ea0729414a78b237563ed2158abc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="dbfa894caa4440bbb265edbed687a788"><span offset-key="dbfa894caa4440bbb265edbed687a788:0">Task: Check to see that all media can be paused.</span></span>

<span key="fd13fa9029944073983a3e9112658a14"><span offset-key="fd13fa9029944073983a3e9112658a14:0">Check to see that all media can be paused.</span></span>

<span key="3e1eb9b91f544489a6b3f08a37346156"><span offset-key="3e1eb9b91f544489a6b3f08a37346156:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/keyboard-operation-keyboard-operable.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6a67f4000e2e46ecb8b9ff7b77dfda58" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="48b6cbd77be64c1495cc902a163d5cbf"><span data-offset-key="48b6cbd77be64c1495cc902a163d5cbf:0">2.1.1 KEYBOARD</span></span></span></a><span key="5acb32ef7da14b13ac7984ad725865f9"><span offset-key="5acb32ef7da14b13ac7984ad725865f9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="fe5adb7e7bf4450e944bd783191a3d27"><span offset-key="fe5adb7e7bf4450e944bd783191a3d27:0">Provide a global pause function on any media element. If the device has a keyboard, ensure that pressing the </span>`Space`<span offset-key="fe5adb7e7bf4450e944bd783191a3d27:2"> key can pause playback. Make sure you also don't interfere with the </span>`Space`<span offset-key="fe5adb7e7bf4450e944bd783191a3d27:4"> key's ability to scroll the page/view when not focusing on a form control.</span></span>

<span key="68480ef8b2ef42ffaddfc60687d9df4c"><span offset-key="68480ef8b2ef42ffaddfc60687d9df4c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-to-see-that-all-media-can-be-paused" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="424c638219754a888227f6b023ed5680" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0421b935f6124fb2b86d0488bf8ee4a7"><span data-offset-key="0421b935f6124fb2b86d0488bf8ee4a7:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK TO SEE THAT ALL MEDIA CAN BE PAUSED.</span></span></span></a><span key="ab82ecc6a43343acae44adf86b10415c"><span offset-key="ab82ecc6a43343acae44adf86b10415c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="3b61ff380eb5418a851b0b6bcb789896"><span offset-key="3b61ff380eb5418a851b0b6bcb789896:0">Video</span></span>

<span key="99b409f1ad3f45d0890ac9a8726ef038"><span offset-key="99b409f1ad3f45d0890ac9a8726ef038:0">Video-specific checks.</span></span>

<span key="6b0a08231e6d46cf8cb15955a78c98cf"><span offset-key="6b0a08231e6d46cf8cb15955a78c98cf:0">Task: Confirm the presence of captions.</span></span>

<span key="3981c8b14d3041679e7f99ba1df89a75"><span offset-key="3981c8b14d3041679e7f99ba1df89a75:0">Confirm the presence of captions.</span></span>

<span key="59369f29888040279877582816af4c16"><span offset-key="59369f29888040279877582816af4c16:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/media-equiv-captions.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a44bfc1027da4cd6a6b31b48c421eb20" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="51b108dc23b94a369a390c045bcbb39a"><span data-offset-key="51b108dc23b94a369a390c045bcbb39a:0">1.2.2 CAPTIONS</span></span></span></a><span key="d5c69c6029634d92ae0df63031cea186"><span offset-key="d5c69c6029634d92ae0df63031cea186:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="912db36b7c3e4d528c8e4bd03eb2aad8"><span offset-key="912db36b7c3e4d528c8e4bd03eb2aad8:0">Captions allow a person who cannot hear the audio content of a video to still understand its content.</span></span>

<span key="5ec74164b87240cb83071fbf8f8addfc"><span offset-key="5ec74164b87240cb83071fbf8f8addfc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#confirm-the-presence-of-captions" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a137ac6a217a43be811ac873e70782d8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="775e8e90d4df4a72b37bf79de1a9bcef"><span data-offset-key="775e8e90d4df4a72b37bf79de1a9bcef:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CONFIRM THE PRESENCE OF CAPTIONS.</span></span></span></a><span key="18712b6ceb80447bbff97ff6d79e98b7"><span offset-key="18712b6ceb80447bbff97ff6d79e98b7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="4ed74454272b43c68af5436ee1e6f6fc"><span offset-key="4ed74454272b43c68af5436ee1e6f6fc:0">Task: Remove seizure triggers.</span></span>

<span key="0aedebef1c74403ba6b9cada99e4dea3"><span offset-key="0aedebef1c74403ba6b9cada99e4dea3:0">Remove seizure triggers.</span></span>

<span key="ec301a79ffe14db989855cad4110284f"><span offset-key="ec301a79ffe14db989855cad4110284f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/seizure-does-not-violate.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3df3097cc2bd4d85bacd023060e594e0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="85e0be4b3f81429bb56eba35013a97ca"><span data-offset-key="85e0be4b3f81429bb56eba35013a97ca:0">2.3.1 THREE FLASHES OR BELOW THRESHOLD</span></span></span></a><span key="bcddd8d37ef840c2bf2cc5d3f6059ee6"><span offset-key="bcddd8d37ef840c2bf2cc5d3f6059ee6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="3b6d3305352d47ca86757ba90cb4ede1"><span offset-key="3b6d3305352d47ca86757ba90cb4ede1:0">Certain kinds of strobing or flashing animations will trigger seizures.</span></span>

<span key="75c78361c7404fc98ddd0ca8e83c8566"><span offset-key="75c78361c7404fc98ddd0ca8e83c8566:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#remove-seizure-triggers" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f20ecce53bc94340b944f76f012ece6a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d5c48271ead64e87b3b775887d2cffbf"><span data-offset-key="d5c48271ead64e87b3b775887d2cffbf:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: REMOVE SEIZURE TRIGGERS.</span></span></span></a><span key="3b9ef0631a7b4b8f89524132730ff40f"><span offset-key="3b9ef0631a7b4b8f89524132730ff40f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="f52cbcb04ff2471fb9dddf4577de4b40"><span offset-key="f52cbcb04ff2471fb9dddf4577de4b40:0">Audio</span></span>

<span key="ee76d943ece1487a8f1482f358db2557"><span offset-key="ee76d943ece1487a8f1482f358db2557:0">Audio-specific checks.</span></span>

<span key="580dfe5b005143c98b365aac1209424e"><span offset-key="580dfe5b005143c98b365aac1209424e:0">Task: Confirm that transcripts are available.</span></span>

<span key="90d1dbed3862451b9c3b2d322365fa4b"><span offset-key="90d1dbed3862451b9c3b2d322365fa4b:0">Confirm that transcripts are available.</span></span>

<span key="37ec7552bc924d90bcf26ebac72968eb"><span offset-key="37ec7552bc924d90bcf26ebac72968eb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/text-equiv-all.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="53381a2b17c64771b12bce9b633852b1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="23f0b48f5b5b42e69f11cf87c0cfe754"><span data-offset-key="23f0b48f5b5b42e69f11cf87c0cfe754:0">1.1.1 NON-TEXT CONTENT</span></span></span></a><span key="70160cbdc7f74a2190ba562d712404d9"><span offset-key="70160cbdc7f74a2190ba562d712404d9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b1f30ff8383d4b7ba499e85262c36473"><span offset-key="b1f30ff8383d4b7ba499e85262c36473:0">Transcripts allow people who cannot hear to still understand the audio content. It also allows people to digest audio content at a pace that is comfortable to them.</span></span>

<span key="9a7908ffe4234aeba5a9875bc39d779c"><span offset-key="9a7908ffe4234aeba5a9875bc39d779c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#confirm-that-transcripts-are-available" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="658d01cb723649f08b41b880a0437418" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="1c273a6f9cad4656a238fc696ee1f9e1"><span data-offset-key="1c273a6f9cad4656a238fc696ee1f9e1:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CONFIRM THAT TRANSCRIPTS ARE AVAILABLE.</span></span></span></a><span key="f3c51ad405504a7b8fd70936f566e4be"><span offset-key="f3c51ad405504a7b8fd70936f566e4be:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="270896e8b77c4fd99e242ed04b6b4efa"><span offset-key="270896e8b77c4fd99e242ed04b6b4efa:0">Appearance</span></span>

<span key="d130651f29a14962bc809318e9f603c0"><span offset-key="d130651f29a14962bc809318e9f603c0:0">How your website app content looks in any given situation.</span></span>

<span key="13178bd88b9f4654bad496da3c93ecab"><span offset-key="13178bd88b9f4654bad496da3c93ecab:0">Task: Check your content in specialized browsing modes.</span></span>

<span key="44788d65cf224113887e25eeb13dbbce"><span offset-key="44788d65cf224113887e25eeb13dbbce:0">Check your content in specialized browsing modes.</span></span>

<span key="6ef72fbd7c4b482199d61b7fae347e57"><span offset-key="6ef72fbd7c4b482199d61b7fae347e57:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-without-color.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b73677aec6a4487b89c734e24ce233e2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="36fe4dfb1f2e4fb7969107fe799a2e71"><span data-offset-key="36fe4dfb1f2e4fb7969107fe799a2e71:0">1.4.1 USE OF COLOR</span></span></span></a><span key="60428ba801544bddbfeeda50967651ad"><span offset-key="60428ba801544bddbfeeda50967651ad:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a852f5843da7436c9e97f57a02ac83d2"><span offset-key="a852f5843da7436c9e97f57a02ac83d2:0">Activate </span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/posts/2020-01-23-operating-system-and-browser-accessibility-display-modes/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce3892054ab8403e800226aae5fefa01" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="bf86be63c8ea48c8a42cfb21bf6e7a4d"><span data-offset-key="bf86be63c8ea48c8a42cfb21bf6e7a4d:0">modes such as Windows High Contrast or Inverted Colors</span></span></span></a><span key="8ffd6a7a60c549499298411c0628bbf6"><span offset-key="8ffd6a7a60c549499298411c0628bbf6:0">. Is your content still legible? Are your icons, borders, links, form fields, and other content still present? Can you distinguish foreground content from the background?</span></span>

<span key="912c53a0714b4d94a29dc62f3d7cbc99"><span offset-key="912c53a0714b4d94a29dc62f3d7cbc99:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-your-content-in-specialized-browsing-modes" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="05fbb2dcbade41618778f3b109dc61ca" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="215c6715fe0447c49d09422f859c3fb7"><span data-offset-key="215c6715fe0447c49d09422f859c3fb7:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK YOUR CONTENT IN SPECIALIZED BROWSING MODES.</span></span></span></a><span key="37df37603a3248089602121c05b82f4d"><span offset-key="37df37603a3248089602121c05b82f4d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="967e4dcbbee143068b5ccd1095f4f89c"><span offset-key="967e4dcbbee143068b5ccd1095f4f89c:0">Task: Increase text size to 200%.</span></span>

<span key="16c697d7837f4be2b1cacf110382c944"><span offset-key="16c697d7837f4be2b1cacf110382c944:0">Increase text size to 200%.</span></span>

<span key="6d0ec179427047ffa8cde2afd3b704a7"><span offset-key="6d0ec179427047ffa8cde2afd3b704a7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-scale.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="729d1e763b0b4e94ab52e6d8d14be2d7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="5acbf1a6fb874e4cb4b96590482632b3"><span data-offset-key="5acbf1a6fb874e4cb4b96590482632b3:0">1.4.4 RESIZE TEXT</span></span></span></a><span key="cbfd3e724fb04884a20003d908fead50"><span offset-key="cbfd3e724fb04884a20003d908fead50:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="7cc2f0040fb7498abf7913346212aebc"><span offset-key="7cc2f0040fb7498abf7913346212aebc:0">Is the content still readable? Does increasing the text size cause content to overlap?</span></span>

<span key="e1ecc2001c8e4e999c0c26beb72b3286"><span offset-key="e1ecc2001c8e4e999c0c26beb72b3286:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#increase-text-size-to-200percent" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc9fd09272914797b62c7104063954f7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="5fb27eb1deb3482894a228a79c8e2589"><span data-offset-key="5fb27eb1deb3482894a228a79c8e2589:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: INCREASE TEXT SIZE TO 200%.</span></span></span></a><span key="c651a2c1ccc64715ae86cb4df9ae6ebf"><span offset-key="c651a2c1ccc64715ae86cb4df9ae6ebf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a7f0c26a4d934a19bfc7338c25818c15"><span offset-key="a7f0c26a4d934a19bfc7338c25818c15:0">Task: Double-check that good proximity between content is maintained.</span></span>

<span key="58b879adbacb4178901fb0b435739cef"><span offset-key="58b879adbacb4178901fb0b435739cef:0">Double-check that good proximity between content is maintained.</span></span>

<span key="8918d21773314b2d877fa97f86a3144d"><span offset-key="8918d21773314b2d877fa97f86a3144d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/content-structure-separation-understanding.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f5c71f62841c4383abbc1d443c32162d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="2caad8b942074526b349603706bbe54b"><span data-offset-key="2caad8b942074526b349603706bbe54b:0">1.3.3 SENSORY CHARACTERISTICS</span></span></span></a><span key="4ec6581f0a2c4f4896ba1a885578e969"><span offset-key="4ec6581f0a2c4f4896ba1a885578e969:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="632f92807e324be9acee3b8c10aaaea1"><span offset-key="632f92807e324be9acee3b8c10aaaea1:0">Use </span></span><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=S1j6CYT3kWA&amp;feature=youtu.be" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f79820ae4ab4bbd9a27700d864f243f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="c948421bfdff472d892ed241f46c506e"><span data-offset-key="c948421bfdff472d892ed241f46c506e:0">the straw test</span></span></span></a><span key="6f93dc1f477e4ae28a99113d7adc3376"><span offset-key="6f93dc1f477e4ae28a99113d7adc3376:0"> to ensure people who depend on screen zoom software can still easily discover all content.</span></span>

<span key="89e8996afff74fbe85cab5e8ec5d0474"><span offset-key="89e8996afff74fbe85cab5e8ec5d0474:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#double-check-that-good-proximity-between-content-is-maintained" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="550ace7498154d339334450f8b4b777f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7d8b8d1e6e614367ac18d02abe0b62c2"><span data-offset-key="7d8b8d1e6e614367ac18d02abe0b62c2:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: DOUBLE-CHECK THAT GOOD PROXIMITY BETWEEN CONTENT IS MAINTAINED.</span></span></span></a><span key="8c2d31df142d4ea8964c2d2d8fbeba80"><span offset-key="8c2d31df142d4ea8964c2d2d8fbeba80:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="70bf29390d5b42009c8c148618cfa79d"><span offset-key="70bf29390d5b42009c8c148618cfa79d:0">Task: Make sure color isn't the only way information is conveyed.</span></span>

<span key="8d9686f5ae4b4ae58209dff9dbffe7b2"><span offset-key="8d9686f5ae4b4ae58209dff9dbffe7b2:0">Make sure color isn't the only way information is conveyed.</span></span>

<span key="d765f0013cb94f86bca93930dc235e92"><span offset-key="d765f0013cb94f86bca93930dc235e92:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-without-color.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="783dfbd109b14f98b921d1a784c7a7dd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="6db72210c35e4705b7cd08f5fb8add79"><span data-offset-key="6db72210c35e4705b7cd08f5fb8add79:0">1.4.1 USE OF COLOR</span></span></span></a><span key="368972ab92dd48e9929587b23ca2dc85"><span offset-key="368972ab92dd48e9929587b23ca2dc85:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b21b7eb1df174f7e8b1ca7ed2020f107"><span offset-key="b21b7eb1df174f7e8b1ca7ed2020f107:0">Can you still see where links are among body content if everything is grayscale?</span></span>

<span key="3e13827572e44304b7921fbbdcd2b6df"><span offset-key="3e13827572e44304b7921fbbdcd2b6df:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-color-isnt-the-only-way-information-is-conveyed" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5a3f1c4a92f642beb06a48578c4dbc28" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="caaa5cab4f3b4ff291b3d948ed047391"><span data-offset-key="caaa5cab4f3b4ff291b3d948ed047391:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE COLOR ISN'T THE ONLY WAY INFORMATION IS CONVEYED.</span></span></span></a><span key="1d6e3059204240cea81d8b2844caf394"><span offset-key="1d6e3059204240cea81d8b2844caf394:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="ce4aa77dbcad4a37ae7b4e391a00bcbe"><span offset-key="ce4aa77dbcad4a37ae7b4e391a00bcbe:0">Task: Make sure instructions are not visual or audio-only.</span></span>

<span key="c0dbd93558f64b908724d1b85e598b75"><span offset-key="c0dbd93558f64b908724d1b85e598b75:0">Make sure instructions are not visual or audio-only.</span></span>

<span key="f8e2f84f12bb48e98d0808201827879e"><span offset-key="f8e2f84f12bb48e98d0808201827879e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/sensory-characteristics.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ed6cc256111442a5a9460fd5eaeeb230" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="abd7fcba2e6847cc8e277745f4fbd774"><span data-offset-key="abd7fcba2e6847cc8e277745f4fbd774:0">1.3.3 SENSORY CHARACTERISTICS</span></span></span></a><span key="ff1b321e15b142f6841fad836b141572"><span offset-key="ff1b321e15b142f6841fad836b141572:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b4a6cd3d7e9f40db9b7374dcc137e67f"><span offset-key="b4a6cd3d7e9f40db9b7374dcc137e67f:0">Use a combination of characteristics to write cues, particularly the actual names of sections and elements, rather than just descriptions like location ("on the right") or audio ("after the tone").</span></span>

<span key="b9b5767007844f17a7bd9618aec82b65"><span offset-key="b9b5767007844f17a7bd9618aec82b65:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-instructions-are-not-visual-or-audio-only" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e4fb71f29fc045009c6a8e8c65ddf0e8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="c3e0aff7f4ee4a0dbb24ed4a91d8d37e"><span data-offset-key="c3e0aff7f4ee4a0dbb24ed4a91d8d37e:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE INSTRUCTIONS ARE NOT VISUAL OR AUDIO-ONLY.</span></span></span></a><span key="2e1d2ce3ed4341b4abe12f639bfd6d35"><span offset-key="2e1d2ce3ed4341b4abe12f639bfd6d35:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="73cae6a944c14ad8bcfb4c50809a5c03"><span offset-key="73cae6a944c14ad8bcfb4c50809a5c03:0">Task: Use a simple, straightforward, and consistent layout.</span></span>

<span key="ae6ebd16974642fbbd63de9833e903e4"><span offset-key="ae6ebd16974642fbbd63de9833e903e4:0">Use a simple, straightforward, and consistent layout.</span></span>

<span key="123e101d9b5e4d819eba8be97a83c90a"><span offset-key="123e101d9b5e4d819eba8be97a83c90a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/reflow.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b1a0bc7f592843a79d32f3e183888989" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3f9690f3765c4477bedc46090fa2af86"><span data-offset-key="3f9690f3765c4477bedc46090fa2af86:0">1.4.10 REFLOW</span></span></span></a><span key="b885b06f4ad6443295ad655165a77a28"><span offset-key="b885b06f4ad6443295ad655165a77a28:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="fc625813cb444216bfc66bfc98c02733"><span offset-key="fc625813cb444216bfc66bfc98c02733:0">A complicated layout can be confusing to understand and use.</span></span>

<span key="a6f802bcedcf4c62ba9332e8f7d3be35"><span offset-key="a6f802bcedcf4c62ba9332e8f7d3be35:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#use-a-simple-straightforward-and-consistent-layout" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c48bdd29e54e42cc9aa72820e6976252" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="1e0c840d8f2349c79618cd3c5906ba41"><span data-offset-key="1e0c840d8f2349c79618cd3c5906ba41:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: USE A SIMPLE, STRAIGHTFORWARD, AND CONSISTENT LAYOUT.</span></span></span></a><span key="3cf8ff569ed4412da803c0c2b7327641"><span offset-key="3cf8ff569ed4412da803c0c2b7327641:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="5a84587b19384396b9fb4a0f7668d221"><span offset-key="5a84587b19384396b9fb4a0f7668d221:0">Animation</span></span>

<span key="4c3ef0a60bd345dca14c0a21c5953a2b"><span offset-key="4c3ef0a60bd345dca14c0a21c5953a2b:0">Content that moves, either on its own, or when triggered by a person activating a control.</span></span>

<span key="01dc428faedc4b889001fe0c992c13eb"><span offset-key="01dc428faedc4b889001fe0c992c13eb:0">Task: Ensure animations are subtle and do not flash too much.</span></span>

<span key="abd782fa60114e2180ab46e5e3faf2b1"><span offset-key="abd782fa60114e2180ab46e5e3faf2b1:0">Ensure animations are subtle and do not flash too much.</span></span>

<span key="b1c395678c7f45f79e818593e63be8b6"><span offset-key="b1c395678c7f45f79e818593e63be8b6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/seizure-does-not-violate.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="725eb179866f4a91aea4a3548c16f705" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="4cc53f5eb6a54262bee7150f9c1fbf6d"><span data-offset-key="4cc53f5eb6a54262bee7150f9c1fbf6d:0">2.3.1 THREE FLASHES OR BELOW THRESHOLD</span></span></span></a><span key="d972d05882bf4f2eb2adaad6d8bfee29"><span offset-key="d972d05882bf4f2eb2adaad6d8bfee29:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="6431ce98d1e545d2973a8e9a51a3057d"><span offset-key="6431ce98d1e545d2973a8e9a51a3057d:0">Certain kinds of strobing or flashing animations will trigger seizures. Others may be distracting and disruptive, especially for certain kinds of cognitive disability such as ADHD.</span></span>

<span key="e9308deca4054a2c8082a7b60870a0db"><span offset-key="e9308deca4054a2c8082a7b60870a0db:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-animations-are-subtle-and-do-not-flash-too-much" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a578130cedd744d2b67a92e7d28b904f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="cfc01df7779e4ad286b80219e1493b0b"><span data-offset-key="cfc01df7779e4ad286b80219e1493b0b:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE ANIMATIONS ARE SUBTLE AND DO NOT FLASH TOO MUCH.</span></span></span></a><span key="d743f876ebb34b1ebff66b08903a5394"><span offset-key="d743f876ebb34b1ebff66b08903a5394:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="20742d5d7a5b43c1aa81fc2ad1473909"><span offset-key="20742d5d7a5b43c1aa81fc2ad1473909:0">Task: Provide a mechanism to pause background video.</span></span>

<span key="323a88acc166417283edb46ba0aa6c38"><span offset-key="323a88acc166417283edb46ba0aa6c38:0">Provide a mechanism to pause background video.</span></span>

<span key="73bbc4e00aee4f7eb2840c23c44b82df"><span offset-key="73bbc4e00aee4f7eb2840c23c44b82df:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/time-limits-pause.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="22bcd9c182ab4a1eaf43a8b211566b9a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="2f468ab9923d4c4eba21c3e7893b521f"><span data-offset-key="2f468ab9923d4c4eba21c3e7893b521f:0">2.2.2 PAUSE, STOP, HIDE</span></span></span></a><span key="0e9cdf8bc63b4211841ff3cacc0191fc"><span offset-key="0e9cdf8bc63b4211841ff3cacc0191fc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="d598f6af283148a099e598ac16c703c2"><span offset-key="d598f6af283148a099e598ac16c703c2:0">Background video can be distracting, especially if content is placed over it.</span></span>
