<span key="b71dd87ff8f24ef18243b655a4d31c23"><span offset-key="b71dd87ff8f24ef18243b655a4d31c23:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#provide-a-mechanism-to-pause-background-video" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="250b9fa4181342628f507107c6454a0a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a7f62b0f4e914a07bc29a1fc52390a36"><span data-offset-key="a7f62b0f4e914a07bc29a1fc52390a36:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: PROVIDE A MECHANISM TO PAUSE BACKGROUND VIDEO.</span></span></span></a><span key="1b8cffd45b3b4489b4c15cf50be2ac7c"><span offset-key="1b8cffd45b3b4489b4c15cf50be2ac7c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="43389e6126474f2bb804d882736ab2c1"><span offset-key="43389e6126474f2bb804d882736ab2c1:0">Task: Make sure all animation obeys the </span>`prefers-reduced-motion`<span offset-key="43389e6126474f2bb804d882736ab2c1:2"> media query.</span></span>

<span key="93d53cc4801a4349a64eec1c76968d4b"><span offset-key="93d53cc4801a4349a64eec1c76968d4b:0">Make sure all animation obeys the </span>`prefers-reduced-motion`<span offset-key="93d53cc4801a4349a64eec1c76968d4b:2"> media query.</span></span>

<span key="bfed612c845441758dbfd44af651d909"><span offset-key="bfed612c845441758dbfd44af651d909:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/animation-from-interactions.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="202a3d3ca05c40b8b092361b98b89300" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="69308d4a85bf4d4da529e0f28c0b5b8a"><span data-offset-key="69308d4a85bf4d4da529e0f28c0b5b8a:0">2.3.3 ANIMATION FROM INTERACTIONS</span></span></span></a><span key="66d273bfc6b94960be48a094f2b537af"><span offset-key="66d273bfc6b94960be48a094f2b537af:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="c34d6f8e5ca3470497918381bfa55022"><span offset-key="c34d6f8e5ca3470497918381bfa55022:0">Remove animations when the "reduce motion" setting is activated. If an animation is necessary to communicate meaning for a concept, slow its duration down.</span></span>

<span key="c657cb2ebc5e41d688a28ef9eee3afd4"><span offset-key="c657cb2ebc5e41d688a28ef9eee3afd4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#make-sure-all-animation-obeys-the-prefers-reduced-motion-media-query" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d64061fdbb234fc0a0dce8c33b87a6cf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0be1645388d94037b2120a033f4e3161"><span data-offset-key="0be1645388d94037b2120a033f4e3161:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: MAKE SURE ALL ANIMATION OBEYS THE </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="0be1645388d94037b2120a033f4e3161:1">PREFERS-REDUCED-MOTION</code><span data-offset-key="0be1645388d94037b2120a033f4e3161:2"> MEDIA QUERY.</span></span></span></a><span key="4130ace4b3d946ef991d85a3620c9db2"><span offset-key="4130ace4b3d946ef991d85a3620c9db2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="1a4fbc4ea3034649837b12daca8a2e18"><span offset-key="1a4fbc4ea3034649837b12daca8a2e18:0">Color contrast</span></span>

<span key="ba41009482754592b56b11320f6cad02"><span offset-key="ba41009482754592b56b11320f6cad02:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/posts/2015-01-05-what-is-color-contrast/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="88fa615571234f4f86777568616df9d2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="8aa401f8d04a48d9a7f8044a12d23ef5"><span data-offset-key="8aa401f8d04a48d9a7f8044a12d23ef5:0">Color contrast</span></span></span></a><span key="2c8998d6d6fc4a698803c828bb08e952"><span offset-key="2c8998d6d6fc4a698803c828bb08e952:0"> is how legible colors are when placed next to, and on top of each other.</span></span>

<span key="30ce77390be74567b73291e903f1bdbd"><span offset-key="30ce77390be74567b73291e903f1bdbd:0">Task: Check the contrast for all normal-sized text.</span></span>

<span key="b5f07afba82e4f9d9407a5139cd48bfe"><span offset-key="b5f07afba82e4f9d9407a5139cd48bfe:0">Check the contrast for all normal-sized text.</span></span>

<span key="adac4213ca134dd49a4e5fbdce2122fb"><span offset-key="adac4213ca134dd49a4e5fbdce2122fb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e0cf3b10608a4630bc9d1e57d17d410d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="a93fd39de8644252887b9b7051ffc190"><span data-offset-key="a93fd39de8644252887b9b7051ffc190:0">1.4.3 CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="174c944cca244907b9e02c8dcf4b1e32"><span offset-key="174c944cca244907b9e02c8dcf4b1e32:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8d751df34d9e45a5881d46568ecca1a1"><span offset-key="8d751df34d9e45a5881d46568ecca1a1:0">Level AA compliance requires a contrast ratio of 4.5:1.</span></span>

<span key="d356a0a40c0d46dbb019fb026f805ed6"><span offset-key="d356a0a40c0d46dbb019fb026f805ed6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-the-contrast-for-all-normal-sized-text" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="566632aa75e946a0a48b2da22776e326" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="5002966208044c7ea685a9d75049b3cc"><span data-offset-key="5002966208044c7ea685a9d75049b3cc:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK THE CONTRAST FOR ALL NORMAL-SIZED TEXT.</span></span></span></a><span key="d10170000b734be2b91883646638996c"><span offset-key="d10170000b734be2b91883646638996c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f0a25ac877784c49979130b28ae34b25"><span offset-key="f0a25ac877784c49979130b28ae34b25:0">Task: Check the contrast for all large-sized text.</span></span>

<span key="c5e7fb0c9f574dc4aa114712a0bfe97d"><span offset-key="c5e7fb0c9f574dc4aa114712a0bfe97d:0">Check the contrast for all large-sized text.</span></span>

<span key="fd553be9419540e39d4d4ad793acb1fa"><span offset-key="fd553be9419540e39d4d4ad793acb1fa:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dcdc5f79ef1e402d8c1bea0610f04ae0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="2e5748086e104b0b91c8aac6fcb30145"><span data-offset-key="2e5748086e104b0b91c8aac6fcb30145:0">1.4.3 CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="05aa6e8a78ed4f6d9867885c6c9ed0f1"><span offset-key="05aa6e8a78ed4f6d9867885c6c9ed0f1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="28ec01bf1ab444ef959e005adb576198"><span offset-key="28ec01bf1ab444ef959e005adb576198:0">Level AA compliance requires a contrast ratio of 3:1.</span></span>

<span key="9be3b0cba7814de4b01e52209aabcb6b"><span offset-key="9be3b0cba7814de4b01e52209aabcb6b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-the-contrast-for-all-large-sized-text" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9a4928ea36ab4c30b089103a6eb57981" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="1716db2e5e8243d3b45b680b376b1494"><span data-offset-key="1716db2e5e8243d3b45b680b376b1494:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK THE CONTRAST FOR ALL LARGE-SIZED TEXT.</span></span></span></a><span key="cdfb620568784da891d7f02a30eb19df"><span offset-key="cdfb620568784da891d7f02a30eb19df:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="e9531e3b34a749be84137dc8bab4c212"><span offset-key="e9531e3b34a749be84137dc8bab4c212:0">Task: Check the contrast for all icons.</span></span>

<span key="fc5490b0699440eda50b1ea205d12251"><span offset-key="fc5490b0699440eda50b1ea205d12251:0">Check the contrast for all icons.</span></span>

<span key="7713d886505f4102a65159791528a618"><span offset-key="7713d886505f4102a65159791528a618:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/non-text-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bf6e536537744729b1166cefb96ff4e8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="227c751fdd7a4ae18cba066b52f1aed1"><span data-offset-key="227c751fdd7a4ae18cba066b52f1aed1:0">1.4.11 NON-TEXT CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="bf1411d066fd46b9aa39f22d7565fea9"><span offset-key="bf1411d066fd46b9aa39f22d7565fea9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="7bb48d3f14c247779fa62c2d1e6df1e4"><span offset-key="7bb48d3f14c247779fa62c2d1e6df1e4:0">Level AA compliance requires a contrast ratio of 3.0:1.</span></span>

<span key="73a3d0075df547db84c0ceff67e88c66"><span offset-key="73a3d0075df547db84c0ceff67e88c66:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-the-contrast-for-all-icons" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e4f5688b71945039c1cc017195ab3ab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="d59f5d9b0e35411d82fb02f26ccb7ac7"><span data-offset-key="d59f5d9b0e35411d82fb02f26ccb7ac7:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK THE CONTRAST FOR ALL ICONS.</span></span></span></a><span key="954aa83c5938419f84053c43624fde47"><span offset-key="954aa83c5938419f84053c43624fde47:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f4e179138f944bbeb0fc3d735ea4c075"><span offset-key="f4e179138f944bbeb0fc3d735ea4c075:0">Task: Check the contrast of borders for input elements (text input, radio buttons, checkboxes, etc.).</span></span>

<span key="d50f766ed1bf4d90b2a764acecf69c61"><span offset-key="d50f766ed1bf4d90b2a764acecf69c61:0">Check the contrast of borders for input elements (text input, radio buttons, checkboxes, etc.).</span></span>

<span key="bd0bbc19cb6d420886868fdc7569c7c2"><span offset-key="bd0bbc19cb6d420886868fdc7569c7c2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/non-text-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd075da539d049f79ffddb81e51d49a4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="aaeb70f3349445f6b6bf8d7635ec4d31"><span data-offset-key="aaeb70f3349445f6b6bf8d7635ec4d31:0">1.4.11 NON-TEXT CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="fbff27ebbfac4fb48c15da3b8b386915"><span offset-key="fbff27ebbfac4fb48c15da3b8b386915:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="3941aed8ee80487ca19186a35cbabcdf"><span offset-key="3941aed8ee80487ca19186a35cbabcdf:0">Level AA compliance requires a contrast ratio of 3.0:1.</span></span>

<span key="d016b95f889f4ab195aaebc5bfe9c4cb"><span offset-key="d016b95f889f4ab195aaebc5bfe9c4cb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-the-contrast-of-borders-for-input-elements-text-input-radio-buttons-checkboxes-etc" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="63b53d4764e64776bf7fd52e3485a21c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="0d3fe0fb7c0748a39fc68232f32711fa"><span data-offset-key="0d3fe0fb7c0748a39fc68232f32711fa:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK THE CONTRAST OF BORDERS FOR INPUT ELEMENTS (TEXT INPUT, RADIO BUTTONS, CHECKBOXES, ETC.).</span></span></span></a><span key="39ed90e86e9646eb8807de3890da661d"><span offset-key="39ed90e86e9646eb8807de3890da661d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5fdfb8bfe7924094931345e03efdd7de"><span offset-key="5fdfb8bfe7924094931345e03efdd7de:0">Task: Check text that overlaps images or video.</span></span>

<span key="7f298ee9ca1e4636bd2e949262ca2782"><span offset-key="7f298ee9ca1e4636bd2e949262ca2782:0">Check text that overlaps images or video.</span></span>

<span key="8926d72e4ad24049873089d3b3c557ef"><span offset-key="8926d72e4ad24049873089d3b3c557ef:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="71d14833559a41e0b08c660998eb7199" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="28b537c2cd9b4e009c5ef90acaf0e8da"><span data-offset-key="28b537c2cd9b4e009c5ef90acaf0e8da:0">1.4.3 CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="d6e61e3d215249b8811fae7f3551ab68"><span offset-key="d6e61e3d215249b8811fae7f3551ab68:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="6781aa5f19d14f198d6a20106cdb4d07"><span offset-key="6781aa5f19d14f198d6a20106cdb4d07:0">Is text still legible?</span></span>

<span key="9bde4e1cb5b643dfa2d29b93438f37d7"><span offset-key="9bde4e1cb5b643dfa2d29b93438f37d7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-text-that-overlaps-images-or-video" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a86a99603ec449de828ebff5f02faadf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="dcb19c98e26d40468a96aaae3c959106"><span data-offset-key="dcb19c98e26d40468a96aaae3c959106:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK TEXT THAT OVERLAPS IMAGES OR VIDEO.</span></span></span></a><span key="14e25def31614a78a21ead852cd0f74b"><span offset-key="14e25def31614a78a21ead852cd0f74b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="73fef10df0c44765b7d20c62f0765a70"><span offset-key="73fef10df0c44765b7d20c62f0765a70:0">Task: Check custom </span>`::selection`<span offset-key="73fef10df0c44765b7d20c62f0765a70:2"> colors.</span></span>

<span key="c9baa81fdd00484881b4cf27d599df86"><span offset-key="c9baa81fdd00484881b4cf27d599df86:0">Check custom </span>`::selection`<span offset-key="c9baa81fdd00484881b4cf27d599df86:2"> colors.</span></span>

<span key="0787c9d8f5ab4a1495105040f6b41a51"><span offset-key="0787c9d8f5ab4a1495105040f6b41a51:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/visual-audio-contrast-contrast.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="25525f3bbd9940589d82e24bb841554f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="68fb1c22ea82430a91fb1dcd3186ddb4"><span data-offset-key="68fb1c22ea82430a91fb1dcd3186ddb4:0">1.4.3 CONTRAST</span></span></span></a><span key="45a5edbaf7a64cf497dc90401fe6ecab"><span offset-key="45a5edbaf7a64cf497dc90401fe6ecab:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="bb9b1b80a73f470ba423f4f8983de20e"><span offset-key="bb9b1b80a73f470ba423f4f8983de20e:0">Is the color contrast you set in your </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/::selection" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="23d8c169b0d044edb2af280319cb0c6d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="398a9476858646a99c3782c52051cdf3"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="398a9476858646a99c3782c52051cdf3:0">::selection</code><span data-offset-key="398a9476858646a99c3782c52051cdf3:1"> CSS declaration</span></span></span></a><span key="0e50cc1717ca4bc4baf047728df24e24"><span offset-key="0e50cc1717ca4bc4baf047728df24e24:0"> sufficient? Otherwise someone may not be able read it if they highlight it.</span></span>

<span key="370c4cf490544d94abc5bcf79253f689"><span offset-key="370c4cf490544d94abc5bcf79253f689:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-custom-selection-colors" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="42636b2f55804da3b047aaa49ab01b75" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="16301430163e47ec80a3b41fe1e27d68"><span data-offset-key="16301430163e47ec80a3b41fe1e27d68:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK CUSTOM </span><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="16301430163e47ec80a3b41fe1e27d68:1">::SELECTION</code><span data-offset-key="16301430163e47ec80a3b41fe1e27d68:2"> COLORS.</span></span></span></a><span key="e8d170cb6db64815905eb9bafba2bd18"><span offset-key="e8d170cb6db64815905eb9bafba2bd18:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="73a5140509e54496977905fdbadf821a"><span offset-key="73a5140509e54496977905fdbadf821a:0">Mobile and touch</span></span>

<span key="0f3c11e288004313bf0e2ef647d1f2f5"><span offset-key="0f3c11e288004313bf0e2ef647d1f2f5:0">Things to check mobile experiences for.</span></span>

<span key="e577301ae3204449b2ea7692eb3c7e55"><span offset-key="e577301ae3204449b2ea7692eb3c7e55:0">Task: Check that the site can be rotated to any orientation.</span></span>

<span key="175eb5f5288a43639c725dc85776ebe6"><span offset-key="175eb5f5288a43639c725dc85776ebe6:0">Check that the site can be rotated to any orientation.</span></span>

<span key="2d6e80185b0946f3b266b44c8e7f1826"><span offset-key="2d6e80185b0946f3b266b44c8e7f1826:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/orientation.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e9bd0f9eb95e4d78b5313d3fd05c4944" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="f899ed43236140a39518af0a1f74d9aa"><span data-offset-key="f899ed43236140a39518af0a1f74d9aa:0">1.3.4 ORIENTATION</span></span></span></a><span key="4494aba2bd2e4abead00737f73ac8ac9"><span offset-key="4494aba2bd2e4abead00737f73ac8ac9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="1cf0c91c5dc44af3a6ea5ab2882675ca"><span offset-key="1cf0c91c5dc44af3a6ea5ab2882675ca:0">Does the site only allow portrait orientation?</span></span>

<span key="1456aeb19d3544638786fdc99b80f890"><span offset-key="1456aeb19d3544638786fdc99b80f890:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#check-that-the-site-can-be-rotated-to-any-orientation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="697baa64dcc242ddbe5ced974b2048be" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7f81a8f76a2747959b51f34958f3cf7e"><span data-offset-key="7f81a8f76a2747959b51f34958f3cf7e:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: CHECK THAT THE SITE CAN BE ROTATED TO ANY ORIENTATION.</span></span></span></a><span key="574f343b425c4c6f80282ff8a2a3113a"><span offset-key="574f343b425c4c6f80282ff8a2a3113a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5573051858ce4273b0ff67fade58b08f"><span offset-key="5573051858ce4273b0ff67fade58b08f:0">Task: Remove horizontal scrolling.</span></span>

<span key="f3db1aa0ae0a4cc48e67fd091795b240"><span offset-key="f3db1aa0ae0a4cc48e67fd091795b240:0">Remove horizontal scrolling.</span></span>

<span key="37e7513a419d4048859fbc0435a8ba64"><span offset-key="37e7513a419d4048859fbc0435a8ba64:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/reflow.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9a6529bb7c8f4cf38a1116798d1c6f49" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="617dca70623144b49e7d0079d8b7f0d3"><span data-offset-key="617dca70623144b49e7d0079d8b7f0d3:0">1.4.10 REFLOW</span></span></span></a><span key="54acc8d0d47c43d5b4056950a9d4716e"><span offset-key="54acc8d0d47c43d5b4056950a9d4716e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5a1ac02874514d838a5cd4bd560429b2"><span offset-key="5a1ac02874514d838a5cd4bd560429b2:0">Requiring someone to scroll horizontally can be difficult for some, irritating for all.</span></span>

<span key="682ed2932fba4fab95c7211f7bd8df76"><span offset-key="682ed2932fba4fab95c7211f7bd8df76:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#remove-horizontal-scrolling" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1dd87382aaa646028de4ecba0b5d1815" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="3143da40a5164d829e0b249fc21d6102"><span data-offset-key="3143da40a5164d829e0b249fc21d6102:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: REMOVE HORIZONTAL SCROLLING.</span></span></span></a><span key="c31a00f96ba2433792ef1a9224d88238"><span offset-key="c31a00f96ba2433792ef1a9224d88238:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="24dc9cb4868a4a7ebbba4941fdc5ffad"><span offset-key="24dc9cb4868a4a7ebbba4941fdc5ffad:0">Task: Ensure that button and link icons can be activated with ease.</span></span>

<span key="5e7963076b284542867cfbb05eec1adc"><span offset-key="5e7963076b284542867cfbb05eec1adc:0">Ensure that button and link icons can be activated with ease.</span></span>

<span key="1e62450a84054aeb8839d7383471a2cf"><span offset-key="1e62450a84054aeb8839d7383471a2cf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/target-size.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="87bd8013cf294f32a1e18efd4b927c78" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="ff62aadc89304c3bae4a04fd4aaeee9b"><span data-offset-key="ff62aadc89304c3bae4a04fd4aaeee9b:0">2.5.5 TARGET SIZE</span></span></span></a><span key="447c5ae6b1c745058827f1e5f954103d"><span offset-key="447c5ae6b1c745058827f1e5f954103d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="22b36e232c8344f4ad70e88af0a7baba"><span offset-key="22b36e232c8344f4ad70e88af0a7baba:0">It's good to make sure things like hamburger menus, social icons, gallery viewers, and other touch controls are usable by a wide range of hand and stylus sizes.</span></span>

<span key="21360d7cc8344c85b6f657c40436ceb5"><span offset-key="21360d7cc8344c85b6f657c40436ceb5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-that-button-and-link-icons-can-be-activated-with-ease" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b829d2afb0144735aecd559b307a8a11" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="7f09c24efb874869bbcf65640e2f1a45"><span data-offset-key="7f09c24efb874869bbcf65640e2f1a45:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE THAT BUTTON AND LINK ICONS CAN BE ACTIVATED WITH EASE.</span></span></span></a><span key="08df4ff26ad4460584671e0c715e2c87"><span offset-key="08df4ff26ad4460584671e0c715e2c87:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="ef18589f7543421bac7a515ecb7d5d4f"><span offset-key="ef18589f7543421bac7a515ecb7d5d4f:0">Task: Ensure sufficient space between interactive items in order to provide a scroll area.</span></span>

<span key="d69db28820864d0eb2009dfaf77c393d"><span offset-key="d69db28820864d0eb2009dfaf77c393d:0">Ensure sufficient space between interactive items in order to provide a scroll area.</span></span>

<span key="dbb613e5bb8d41f9ae046bcd1b0c0d35"><span offset-key="dbb613e5bb8d41f9ae046bcd1b0c0d35:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-skip.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4e5c249008de4c8ab2aae01126e679bc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="819d3ae080a4461e9e10fea9fe837904"><span data-offset-key="819d3ae080a4461e9e10fea9fe837904:0">2.4.1 BYPASS BLOCKS</span></span></span></a><span key="4bf3f7ebc22748b0964a6cd6a0aae74a"><span offset-key="4bf3f7ebc22748b0964a6cd6a0aae74a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f52fb3825f1a4a8fad0ee52dc8caaa8f"><span offset-key="f52fb3825f1a4a8fad0ee52dc8caaa8f:0">Some people who experience motor control issues such as </span></span><a href="https://axesslab.com/hand-tremors/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4ed0cc9ef3134898ab5383faadc76e87" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="c0b88582f7d540a889070db64c84211b"><span data-offset-key="c0b88582f7d540a889070db64c84211b:0">hand tremors</span></span></span></a><span key="ab47a4599cfb44a3af4e861716e9ccb2"><span offset-key="ab47a4599cfb44a3af4e861716e9ccb2:0"> may have a very difficult time scrolling past interactive items which feature zero spacing.</span></span>

<span key="9c47b744a0ef41889960a6c7918822d3"><span offset-key="9c47b744a0ef41889960a6c7918822d3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/checklist/#ensure-sufficient-space-between-interactive-items-in-order-to-provide-a-scroll-area" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e54b73b9202e4475b0862be53fc4aaf1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="cb55b914fc0d45b39ddfccc58277ca22"><span data-offset-key="cb55b914fc0d45b39ddfccc58277ca22:0">SHARE LINKTO CHECKLIST ITEM: ENSURE SUFFICIENT SPACE BETWEEN INTERACTIVE ITEMS IN ORDER TO PROVIDE A SCROLL AREA.</span></span></span></a><span key="752b98c40d354c35b3e653afd1855ea3"><span offset-key="752b98c40d354c35b3e653afd1855ea3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="1deb3098c1104121b33435e4f609defa"><span offset-key="1deb3098c1104121b33435e4f609defa:0">Next steps</span></span>

<span key="bb15a817ea1a4b2bb06bc1cef6ab0ef2"><span offset-key="bb15a817ea1a4b2bb06bc1cef6ab0ef2:0">Remember to periodically check your site to ensure it is still accessible. The A11Y Project also strongly encourages you to verify your testing by </span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/resources/#professional-testers" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1feb5a0c5e0c44b2af38d7a8c8f34185" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-33079_259-33080-237__"><span data-key="15548d6446684c119a020ae9ee010246"><span data-offset-key="15548d6446684c119a020ae9ee010246:0">hiring a professional tester</span></span></span></a><span key="13c2f1aae16f4c8cb85cccec9a5aa421"><span offset-key="13c2f1aae16f4c8cb85cccec9a5aa421:0">.</span></span>
